Beginning January 1 Next Year

Soviet Russia's Second Five-Year Plan

Develop Eastern and Western Siberia and Build Vladivostok

Railways and All Construction Thoroughly Electrified

▲TASS News Agency Berri Dispatch on the 21st: The Soviet Union's second five-year plan, beginning January 1 next year, will focus on the development of Eastern and Western Siberia. This region is larger in area than Germany, France, Italy, and Poland combined, with enormous hydropower and abundant mineral resources, and is extremely important to the Soviet Union's national economy. In the first five-year plan, two coal mines and miner's unions were established in the area. In the next plan, the number will be increased, so that the hydropower of this area can make any industry surpass others. In the future, railways will run through this area for tens of thousands of miles, and all will be powered by electricity. All other construction will be thoroughly

Electrified as the basis. The power plant is named Angarastrai, and its scale is larger than Neprostrai. It consists of many hydroelectric plants scattered over a large area. The Nipo plant generates 20,000,000,000 kilowatt-hours per year. In the second five-year plan, the Angara plant will generate 20,000,000,000 kilowatt-hours, accounting for one-fifth of the total power generation in the Soviet Union. The construction of this project will begin in 1933 and will not be completed until 1942 in the third five-year plan. In addition, there are smaller power plants, such as the Bajato Tian Factory near the Kiriza Fubo Coalfield, with an annual power generation of 5,500,000,000 kilowatt-hours, the Bajarkayee Factory near Irkutsk with the same power generation, the Paidenskoiy Factory, and the Krasnoyarsk Factory on the Yenisei River, all of which are in the Siberian development plan.

The construction of the port of Vladivostok is particularly important. The number of commercial ships entering and leaving the port has greatly increased in recent years. In 1930, there were only 1,025 ships, and in 1931, the number increased to 2,233. This year, due to other factors, the result will be a tour of the port, but because of the increase in wood transport, traffic to Sakhalin and Kamchatka has also increased. It is expected that it will not be below the record of 1927-29. The port of Vladivostok is now developing rapidly and becoming an independent port. In the past, Siberia was undeveloped, and the port relied entirely on the Chinese Eastern Railway for sustenance. However, the current situation has changed, and the port can now break away from the Chinese Eastern Railway and become independent. The port of Vladivostok was established in 1860, but it did not develop until the construction of the Siberian Railway and the Chinese Eastern Railway in the 19th century. Its special value is that it does not freeze for three months each year. Ten years ago, the Japanese army and the White Russians occupied the area. After they withdrew, construction gradually flourished. This year, there are many factories and schools, making it the industrial and cultural center of Eastern and Western Siberia. The Soviet Union's Pacific merchant fleet is based in Vladivostok. The fleet has 37 ships with a tonnage of approximately 85,000, but this amount is not enough to meet the needs of the port's commerce, so foreign ships are also allowed to enter and leave, most of which are Japanese ships, as well as Chinese and Norwegian ships. The sailors are mostly Chinese. Since the establishment of direct air links between Vladivostok and Moscow, the port has become more important. From Berri to the port, the

The Ussuri Railway will be built with double tracks and will be connected to the railroads to Ugornaya, Gangus, Suchin, Nagoda, Transbaikalia, and Heihe. Many Chinese workers in Vladivostok are doing their best for socialist construction. Most of them are no longer illiterate.

Britain and France Decide to Again Request the United States to Suspend War Debt Payments

MacDonald and Herriot Convene Cabinet Meetings

To Study the Nature of the Reply to the US Government

The Impact of War Debts on the World Economy

▲Reuters, London, 27th: British Prime Minister MacDonald and Chancellor of the Exchequer Chamberlain rushed back to London today to attend cabinet discussions on how to respond to the United States regarding the war debt issue. The British government acknowledges that what is urgently needed is to quickly end the current uncertain state of affairs and immediately submit a well-reasoned application to the United States, in order to persuade the United States to agree to suspend the war debt payment due on December 15. In addition, they are also preparing various statistics to show the impact on the economy after the payment on November 15, in order to summarize and inform the United States. German Engineer Studies Rockets

Using Alcohol and Oxygen as Power

Can Carry One Person to Try Ascending the Sky

▲National Press, Magdeburg, 27th: German engineer Nibel has been studying rockets for many years. He announced today that he will build a rocket that can carry a person to try ascending the sky next spring. If it is successful at that time, it will create a new record in the history of rockets and open a new record in the flying world. Nibel hopes that the rocket will rise to a height of 3,000 feet, and then the passenger will jump off with a parachute. If the experiment is successful, a larger rocket will be made, which is expected to reach a height of 13 miles. No gunpowder is used in the rocket. It uses an explosive liquid made of alcohol and oxygen as power. Half of the cost of manufacturing and research over the years is borne by local authorities, and half is donated by friends. The people and authorities here are also paying close attention to the progress of Nibel's work. In recent Sundays, countless enthusiastic people have often gone to Nibel's residence in the suburbs to visit or listen to Nibel's explanations.

Each debtor country is jointly solving the problem. According to the New York Observer, France's decision will almost certainly shift with Britain. The difficulties France faces are not like Britain's difficulties in exchange rates, but in finding funds is not easy because the French budget is already severely short. Russo-Polish Non-Aggression Treaty Ratified

▲Havas, Warsaw, 27th: The non-aggression treaty and reconciliation agreement between Poland and Soviet Russia have been ratified by order of the Polish President. The constitution does not explicitly stipulate the presidential ratification of treaties. The various treaties listed in the constitution that must be ratified by parliament do not explicitly include non-aggression treaties. Polish jurists believe that only treaties that involve national finances and compel the country to take certain actions must be submitted to parliament for review. Non-aggression treaties are purely negative promises and are therefore not included in the above-mentioned treaties. According to the Polish government, the non-aggression treaty may not be submitted to parliament, and most members were originally prepared to pass this treaty. However, after the negotiations between Romania and Soviet Russia broke down, Polish officials wanted to settle the matter as soon as possible, so they adopted the procedure of presidential ratification.

▲National Press, Warsaw, 28th: Newspapers related to the government today issued special editions welcoming the final ratification of the Russo-Polish non-aggression treaty, saying that Poland's international position can be further consolidated as a result. Several newspapers deeply regretted that Romania had not concluded a similar treaty with Soviet Russia, saying that this move could make peace in Eastern Europe more stable.

German Political System

Schleicher Forms Cabinet in Negotiations

The Greatest Mission of the Federal President

Hitler's Influence Gradually Declines

▲National Press, Berlin, 28th: The call for a successor to the German Chancellor is still concentrated on General Schleicher. It is generally expected that, as with the current truce negotiations between the new cabinet and the parliament, if it can succeed, Schleicher's premiership can be practically determined on Monday or Tuesday. At present, the negotiations are being carried out under high pressure, with the intention of adjourning the parliament until December next year. Schleicher will also talk with the Catholic and Socialist trade unions, because if Schleicher forms a cabinet, he will concentrate his efforts on the unemployment problem, so in order to seek the stability of the government, he must have the support of these two trade union factions. If Schleicher's move is unsuccessful, the final way out of the political situation, it is expected that the president will re-appoint Papen to form a cabinet and dissolve the new parliament.

▲Havas, Berlin, 27th: We have gained a great benefit from the political situation in Germany in recent days, that is, the greatest mission of the Federal President in German politics is clear from this line of action. In the midst of internal chaos in Germany, the Federal President is the only pillar in the stream. Germany, a large country with a population of 60 million, is destined by the head of state's final word. The whole country is in awe and looks to Hindenburg's lead, which is also very different. The remarks of German reporter Hans Zehrer have always been regarded as representing the views of Defense Minister Schleicher. In view of Hindenburg's high age of 80, he is very worried about this phenomenon. Hindenburg has reached the age of decline. If he suddenly falls ill, the authority of the country may go with it. If Hitler is elected as the Federal President in the future, he should not be allowed to have the same power as Hindenburg. After the establishment of the new authoritarian cabinet, its main task is this point. At present, it is naturally impossible to talk about amending the constitution, because if you want to amend the constitution, you must implement a "coup", and Hindenburg is unwilling to use this method. However, since the presidential election law is not stipulated in the constitution, it can be amended by order of the law. In this regard, or a new law can be stipulated, the Federal President may designate a candidate for the successor President before the end of his term or in his will, and the House of Representatives may also elect another person as the second candidate by an absolute majority, and when the people vote to elect a new president, they will choose between these two. If the presidential election law is amended in this way, the immediate effect that can occur is roughly as follows: except that the Hitler Party has an absolute majority of seats in the House of Representatives, Hitler has no possibility of being elected as a presidential candidate by the House. However, if the Xi Party occupies an absolute majority in the House, there is no other way to prevent Hitler from taking power except by force. The struggle in German politics is unclear at present, but its relationship is very important. You can imagine the intentions of all parties on amending the presidential election law.

▲National Press, Berlin, 28th: Yesterday, city elections were held in the cities and towns of Bremen and other cities. The voters of the middle class parties increased by 10% compared with the recent general elections, the National Socialist Party decreased by 22%, and the Social Democratic Party decreased by 8%. Although this matter is not very relevant, it is also very noteworthy.

▲ Reuters, Detroit, 27th - Automotive magnate Ford underwent surgery for a hernia on Saturday and Sunday. His recovery is progressing well, and he slept soundly last night. Doctors are satisfied with his progress. Ford is currently resting in the Ford Hospital, to which he donated US$10 million. As Ford is in his seventies, the surgery is naturally a matter of great concern. Therefore, his friends and relatives are still anxious.

Trotsky Speaks in Copenhagen

Indirectly Makes Peace Overtures to Stalin

Broadcast to the United States by Radio

▲ Reuters, Copenhagen, 28th - Trotsky lectured on communism here last night, and his speech was broadcast to the United States by radio. The fee Trotsky received for his lecture was more than double the highest fee for transatlantic broadcasts. A large contingent of police guarded the venue during Trotsky's lecture.

▲ National News Agency, Copenhagen, 28th - In his speech here, Trotsky did not attack the Moscow authorities. He only praised the communist system and its industrial progress, contrasting it with the current state of capitalist countries, leaving the judgment of superiority or inferiority to the audience. Finally, he indirectly proposed peace overtures to Stalin, declaring that he was ready to return to the country at any time, as he always wanted to be a radical. There were no disturbances in the hall during the speech, but there was not much applause.

▲ National News Agency, Oslo, 28th - The Norwegian government has refused entry to Trotsky and his family.

▲ Reuters, Stockholm, 28th - Trotsky's tour of the Baltic states is said to have caused anxiety among the Soviet authorities. Trotsky is currently in Denmark and plans to visit Lund University in December. Trotsky's brand of communism differs from that of the Russian authorities, which led to his exile in 1928. However, his influence is still feared by the opposition.

World Cotton Harvest

This Year is the Lowest in Nine Years

▲ National News Agency, Washington, 27th - The US Department of Agriculture announced today that this year's world cotton harvest will be the lowest in nearly nine years. This is because the acreage planted with cotton in the United States has been sharply reduced, and the cessation of cotton cultivation in Egypt is even more significant. It has been predicted that cotton production will decrease by 33%. Therefore, even though the cotton harvest in Brazil, Mexico, and Lower India is estimated to reach 4.2 million bales, an increase of 800,000 bales compared to the previous year, and there has also been an increase in cotton production in China and Persia, the estimated global production is only 23.4 million bales. Among them, the US harvest will be between 11 million and 12 million bales. In 1923, the world cotton harvest was 19.125 million bales. The following year, it suddenly increased to 23.825 million bales. Since then, the surplus has accumulated daily, and cotton prices have plummeted. This is the first sharp reduction in nearly nine years.

Important News

Japanese Militarists Again Attempt to Invade Beiping and Tianjin

▲ Using the Su Bingwen Incident as a Pretext

▲ Claiming It Is Related to Zhang Xueliang

Japanese Newspapers Vigorously Promote Disturbances in North China

According to the Osaka Asahi Shimbun, "Our side (the Japanese side) has repeatedly contacted Su Bingwen, but Su Bingwen has refused to meet. Our military believes that the anti-Japanese forces in the Xing'an Mountains will put up a stubborn resistance, and will take resolute measures against the Soviet army. The military is currently studying concrete plans. One aspect is the issue of the residents of Manchuria who are prohibited from residing in the area. When Koiso, the chief of staff of the Kwantung Army, returned to Beijing a few days ago, he discussed the matter carefully with the military authorities. The military authorities are willing to sacrifice the banned residents, but the Ministry of Foreign Affairs is extremely reluctant and still asks the military to discuss a comprehensive plan. However, a new problem has now arisen, namely, evidence of a connection between Su Bingwen's troops and Zhang Xueliang. Therefore, in order to eradicate all anti-Japanese volunteer armies resisting in Manchuria, Zhang Xueliang, who is entrenched in Beiping, is considered harmful to the security of Manchuria. In addition to issuing a major warning in advance, there will be a direct attack on North China."

The Nagoya Shimbun published an editorial on the 22nd, stating that according to Koiso, the chief of staff of the Kwantung Army, who returned to Changchun from Tokyo, during his transit through Seoul, Korea, he told a newspaper reporter, "Su Bingwen does not seem to have any intention of repenting, and a peaceful solution is almost impossible." However, the major problem facing our army is that we do not want to sacrifice the lives of our citizens, but it is quite difficult to rescue them. Su Bingwen's guilt lies in the fact that he disregarded our repeated advice and did not respond to our army's demands. How is Zhang Xueliang to blame? Zhang Xueliang in Beiping and Su Bingwen in northern Manchuria seem to be in contact. If Su Bingwen did not have Zhang Xueliang's support, he would certainly not dare to resist for a long time. Therefore, the Kwantung Army has no choice but to resolve the Zhang Xueliang issue. When the Lytton Investigation Team arrived in China, they actually received a secret report from Ma Zhanshan. This time, the League of Nations is discussing the Lytton Report, which was again obstructed by Su Bingwen. These two major planned actions are undoubtedly instigated by Zhang Xueliang. In order to maintain the security of Manchuria in the future, we must have a resolute determination. During the Manchurian Incident, the Jinzhou government was defeated by our army, and Zhang Xueliang's forces retreated to the west of Shanhaiguan. Now, in order to resolve the security of northern Manchuria, our army has no choice but to attack North China in the end. Otherwise, in the future, there will inevitably be a second and third Ma Zhanshan and a second and third Su Bingwen, and how can the security of Manchuria be completed?"

Manzhouli

Japanese Consul Yamazaki's Report on the Incident Diary (Continued)

(October 3rd) At 10:00 AM, Deputy Zheng visited and reported on the situation of Uno and Kohara, and said that the headquarters intended to send the list of people sheltered in the Jiang Consulate and missing persons to the headquarters for reference. This official sent the above list and entrusted him to inquire about the protection and news of the residents in Hailar, Yilekede, and Duranor.

(October 4th) An anti-Japanese demonstration broke out, with 400 primary school students joining. Led by a music team, they went straight to the consulate and gave anti-Japanese speeches. The atmosphere was very high. A slogan of "Down with Japan" was posted on the consulate's gate. Shortly after, Lieutenant Colonel Liang handed over a receipt for 1,000 yuan received from Dayang by the Hailar dispatch officer. At this time, I learned that the Hailar residents and the two dispatch officers in the consulate, Yamakita and Torisu, were safe and sound. On the other hand, I negotiated with Lieutenant Colonel Yezhong to crack down on the Chinese people's demonstration. At 6:00 PM, Constable Yanzaki was escorted back to the consulate by the headquarters.

(October 5th) The food stored in the consulate is gradually running out, and white rice in the city has also been sold out. I reported to Deputy Peng to do his best and managed to get some adzuki beans and vegetables. At the same time, food and clothing were sent to the imprisoned police officers. Also, because the cash had run out, I borrowed money from the Russian consul for the second time. At 5:00 PM, resident Miyabe Kumahei came to the consulate and requested to negotiate with the headquarters as soon as possible for the detained Japanese.

(October 6th) At 10:30 AM, I received a call from the Russian consul, who had obtained permission from the Railway Protection Army Headquarters to send cash. I then bought some snacks and sent them to the police officers.

(October 7th) At noon, a plane of our army flew over the consulate to scout the situation. The evacuees were extremely happy. At 12:20 PM, Russian Consul Smirnov and Secretary Masgaryan visited, and the headquarters translated Russian.

(October 9th) In the morning, Major General Peng and others wore armbands with red and black colors, with the four characters "Iron-Blooded Save the Country" written on white cloth. On this day, I heard that some residents were sick due to incomplete accommodation in the evacuation area and the lack of sanitary materials, making treatment difficult. Fortunately, two of the police officers' wives were nurses and helped with the diagnosis and treatment.

(October 10th) It was the Double Tenth Festival in China. There was no special performance in the city, but the headquarters held a celebration meeting, which Major General Peng also attended. On this day, I urged the headquarters to allow residents to withdraw and asked the Russian consul for a third loan.

(October 11th) The headquarters ordered me to attend a meeting, but I declined due to illness. On the other hand, I entrusted Major General Peng to investigate whether there were any rice merchants in the city who could buy white rice, but it was difficult to start. I had no choice but to buy 20 bags of flour.

(October 12th) The horses in the consulate were all escaped by both Chinese and Russian people since the incident occurred, and the feed was sufficient. I entrusted Commander Ingerling to take care of them. Soon, I received a telegram from the Soviet consul, saying that there was a shortage of cash and only 400 yuan in taxes were sent. However, the weather was getting colder, and the detained residents and the women in the shelter were suffering from a lack of bedding. I bought 100 bundles of straw and 6 pieces of coarse cloth for temporary use.

(October 13th) In the afternoon, the installation of cold-proof equipment was completed.

(October 14th) On this day, 30 to 40 wounded and sick soldiers were sent from the Xing'an Mountains, and 284 soldiers were transported to Hailar. It was rumored that there was a conflict between Zhalantun and the Japanese army. At 2:00 PM, the Soviet consul called and said that he had telegraphed the Moscow government about the meeting on the 7th and informed Japanese Councilor Amakasu.

(October 15th) At 11:00 AM, Lieutenant Colonel Liang and Director Guo came to the consulate and entrusted me to expedite the purchase of white rice to relieve the residents.

(October 16th) It was rumored in the city that Japanese planes bombed Hailar on the morning of the 15th, injuring innocent people.

(October 18th) This is the order to prohibit the removal of food from Hailar. Also, from the mouths of the Russians who repaired the houses in the consulate, I learned that on the 15th, Hailar was attacked by Japanese military aircraft, and three bombs were dropped. Forty miles of the railway in the rear of Qiqihar have been damaged. On this day, the president of the local Chamber of Commerce and Shaojiang Zhao went to Hailar to discuss the expenses with Su Bingli. On the other hand, the Chinese Self-Defense Corps was organized in the city and trained at the White Russian Middle School. There were about 300 members.

(October 19th) The headquarters raised funds from the shops in the city, and the Russians spread rumors that the Japanese army would come.

(October 20th) I telegraphed the Japanese Embassy in Moscow through the Soviet consul, and begged Commander Ingerling to release the residents and provide food as soon as possible.

(October 22nd) Through negotiations with the Soviet consul, the withdrawal of unrelated residents has been agreed to, and a train is prepared to transport them.

(October 23rd) A general meeting of the evacuees was held to discuss relief measures. I am willing to go back to China with the consul to mediate relief.

(October 24th) At 10:30 AM, the Soviet consul notified by telephone that the first batch of residents to be evacuated would be women and children, and the second batch would be men, but Japanese who were able to fight and those who served in the "Manchukuo" organs would not be allowed to withdraw. Therefore, I quickly compiled a list of women and men's groups and provided them to the Soviet consul in order to obtain permission from the Railway Protection Army Headquarters.

Bombings Occur in Tianjin for Days

Tianjin Correspondence: Bombings have occurred in Tianjin for the past two or three months. The inside story is mostly related to the sale of Japanese goods. North China has always been a major distribution center for Japanese goods. Merchants are profit-oriented, and the municipal government's relentless crackdown on anti-Japanese movements has emboldened them to place orders enthusiastically. Most of these goods are disguised with Western trademarks to deceive people. Patriotic youths are deeply resentful. On the night of the 14th of this month, after bombs exploded simultaneously at the Heji Bicycle Shop on Fourth Road in the French Concession and the Yuda Foreign Cloth Store behind the Yong'an Hotel in Henghe Lane, explosions occurred again on the previous two nights. It is estimated that at about 6:00 PM on the 24th, a young man suddenly placed a cloth-wrapped bomb in an old vacant room in the Lao Zhongji Hardware Store at the south entrance of Nanxie Street, at the intersection of the Chinese and Japanese concessions. The workers there suspected something was wrong and immediately informed the police, who went to the location of the package to investigate. Fortunately, it did not explode. At the same time, when the Guanchang Cloth Store on Beima Road was open for business, a young man suddenly came and threw a bomb in from the upper right. The store's employees quickly avoided it and were not injured. Similar incidents also occurred at the Zhengda Foreign Cloth Store across from the Wanshou Palace in the store and at a cotton yarn store in Xiaohongqiao. At about 8:00 PM, a cloth-wrapped bomb was suddenly found between the doors and windows of the Chengji Paper Store at No. 24 in the French Concession. Because a customer who was buying goods saw it first, it did not explode. At the same time, a young man also threw a bomb at the Yuanfaxiang Cloth Store next to the Datong Shop on Xima Road (placing it in a bucket in front of the store), destroying five pieces of glass. Last night (the 25th) at about 7:00 PM, a young man suddenly threw a bomb into the Changshengyu Paint Store on Beima Road in the Chinese Concession. There was a loud bang, which resounded throughout the city. The store's four glass doors facing the street and the glass door on the front wall, which was about ten feet away, were damaged, and two employees, Ma Dingsan and apprentice Si Rutan, were injured. They were immediately sent to the Municipal Hospital for treatment. It is said that their lives are not in danger. At that time, all the shops in the nearby Gu Yi Street and Needle Street closed their doors to avoid danger. Japanese goods stores were especially fearful. The police sub-station in charge temporarily announced martial law and checked pedestrians. More than an hour and a half later, a sub-grenade was suddenly thrown from the veranda on the fourth floor of the Hengyi Foreign Cloth Store in the Tianxiang Market in the French Concession. The store's manager, Yang Wenjin, and accountant, Jia Tongquan, were both injured in the head and sent to the Xikai French Hospital for treatment. The entire venue was in chaos, and the cries were very loud. The Municipal Public Security Bureau held an emergency meeting today to discuss prevention measures due to the discovery of explosives in the city, which is related to public safety. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the National Salvation Association of Merchants and Citizens are also scheduled to convene merchants dealing in Japanese goods to discuss thorough elimination measures. However, whether this can actually be achieved still depends on whether the merchants have a real awakening. (December 26th)

Liu Zhennian's Troops are Stationed in Fujian

▲ Chen Jiliang Inspected the Navy in Fujian for Days

Fuzhou Correspondence: Regarding the transfer of Liu Zhennian's troops to Fujian and Zhejiang, the Provincial Government received a telegram from the Ministry of Military Affairs a few days ago, stating that Shouning, Zhenghe, Songxi, and Pucheng, which border northern Fujian and eastern Zhejiang, have been designated as their defense area. In addition to the division commander sending personnel to negotiate, please order the governments of the respective counties to take care of Liu's division when they arrive. According to a certain senior military agency, Liu's entire division has more than 18,000 people. Approximately 12,000 people will enter Fujian, board ships in Yantai, and land in Wendeng. Then, they will take the route through Pingyang and Taishun counties to enter Shouning. However, the four counties of Shou, Zheng, Song, and Pu are narrow and the people are poor, so it may be difficult to accommodate this large army. In the future, Pingshan and Fu'an counties will also be assigned to their garrison. The Second Brigade of the Marine Corps, led by Lin Chengchou, is planned to be transferred to Fuding, Xiapu, and Ningde counties along the coast, to form a line with the First Brigade of the Marine Corps, led by Yang Tingying, which is currently stationed in Luoyuan, Lianjiang, and Changle counties. However, it has not yet been designated where the Fourth Brigade of the Provincial Defense Army, led by Xu Yuguang, which is currently stationed in the three counties of Pu, Zheng, and Song, will be transferred. As for whether Liu's division will be under the control of the Pacification Office after entering Fujian, it is not yet known because no orders have been received from the Military Commission. Chen Jiliang, Deputy Minister of the Navy and Commander of the First Fleet, came to Fujian to inspect the fleet. On the 17th, he arrived in Fuzhou from Xiamen on the Haichou warship and anchored at Mawei. In recent days, he has inspected the various forts at the mouth of the Min River, Changmen, Jinpai, and Yutou Niuqiu, as well as the four warships stationed near Mawei, Datong, Ziqiang, Tongji, and Yongxu, as well as the Mawei Shipyard Naval Academy. He is now ordering the troops of the First Brigade of the Marine Corps, which is stationed in Fuzhou, to take turns to Mawei for inspection. He will take a ship to Sandu in the next few days and order the troops of the Second Brigade of the Marine Corps, which are stationed in Funing, to take turns to the area for inspection, and then return to Beijing. However, there have been rumors that Yang Shuzhuang and Chen Shaokuan jointly guarantee Chen Jiliang to succeed as the chairman of the Fujian Provincial Government. Yang Shuzhuang telegraphed Chen Peikun to Shanghai yesterday to discuss this matter, but Chen strongly denied it. (November 23rd)

Kunshan

▲ Master and Servant Lovers Conspire to Kill Husband, Lu Jiaqiao, Kunshan County

Sun, the wife of Li Zhengmei, a private school teacher in Xiaoren Tang, is in her forties and is still very flirtatious. She had an affair with the farmhand Zhou Hexin. Li was always weak and allowed it even though he knew about it. However, Sun and Zhou were still not satisfied. The night before, Zhou Hexin invited Wu Abao and Zhao Qiaosheng to Li's house and smothered him to death with a quilt. Fearing that they would be discovered, they waited until Li was dead before hanging the body on the beam to make it look like suicide, in an attempt to cover it up. The next morning, Sun pretended that her husband had committed suicide and cried bitterly. Neighbors went to watch. Li's uncle also got the news and rushed to the scene. Seeing the marks of a hemp rope on the deceased's neck, he knew that it was a murder. He immediately arrested Sun and the accomplices Zhou Hexin, Wu Abao, Zhao Qiaosheng, and others and sent them to the county government on the 27th to await the dispatch of personnel to verify the matter and deal with it according to law.

Ding refused to accept the sentence and appealed to the Suzhou High Court. The Criminal First Court opened the trial yesterday (28th) afternoon.

▲ Petty Thief Beaten to Death, The Dan Changji Rice Store in Shihuizha, Beizhakou, is run by the brothers Dan Nianhua. More than ten days ago, a red pill addict, Yang A'gen (nicknamed White-Eyed A'gen), sneaked into the store to steal copper spoons, shovels, and other items. The store clerk discovered it and tied up Yang A'gen with a rope and beat him severely. Then, he sent him to the watchman and locked him with a large iron chain. However, Yang A'gen had long been skinny and weak from his addiction to red pills. After being beaten, his injuries were so severe that he was dying. Later, the store clerk and the watchman carried him to an empty boat that was being repaired on the shore nearby. However, A'gen died of his injuries in the early morning of the previous day. The boat owner found out and, fearing that he would be implicated, immediately carried the body to the ground. Later, Peng Xiwu, Director of the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau in charge of the area, learned about it. Because the case involved human life, he sent the police to arrest the watchman and informed Wu Jiahe, the chief of the Fourth District of the area, to report to the County Court for an autopsy.

▲ Automobile Dispute Re-emerges, The decision of the Jiangyin County Party and government talk meeting to allow small cars to run eight trips a day and issue flags by the Jiangyin Construction and Public Security Bureaus seems to have come to an end. The representatives of the small car company, Shi Qinglin and others, took a small car to Jiangyin County a few days ago to get the flag. Therefore, it has sent personnel to Cheng to investigate and negotiate everything with the long-distance bus company.

▲ Detective Plans to Capture Robber, The County Police Squad Detective Liao Dajin received a secret report from an informant that two robbers, Wang Mingshan and Liu Changlian, who had robbed the Dan Changji Rice Store and the Xiehe Lumber Store, were hiding in Pudong and Yidaizhijiao in Shanghai. Zhenjiang

▲ Yong Tai Chang Copper and Tin Shop Ceases Business for Liquidation. Yong Tai Chang Copper and Tin Shop, located at the entrance of Wan Jia Alley, was established as a partnership by the Yang and Tong families. It had been operating successfully for several years, accumulating profits of over ten thousand in the past two years and gaining a strong reputation. Consequently, it attracted deposits totaling around twenty thousand yuan, mostly belonging to widows and orphans as their means of survival, or to elderly people for funeral expenses. The highest monthly interest rate was 1.2%, while the lowest was 0.6% or 0.7%. However, at the end of October, rumors of instability and planned liquidation spread. This caused a rush of withdrawals. A certain gentleman intervened, proposing a three-year moratorium on principal repayments, with only interest payments to be made to maintain operations and prevent losses for both parties. The majority of depositors agreed, and the business continued to operate. Unexpectedly, it suddenly announced its closure the other day, hiring a lawyer to handle the liquidation. It is estimated that the shortfall in deposits and outstanding accounts amounts to over twenty thousand yuan, while the inventory and assets are said to be worth only five thousand gold, and are already being liquidated. Creditors held a special meeting yesterday to organize a creditor group to investigate the accounts, and plan to prosecute if any irregularities are found.

▲ Sixteen-Year-Old Boy Rapes Young Girl. Yu Chunhua from Shuyang, who makes a living as a rickshaw puller in this city, resides in the Huo巷 Alley in the city. His wife, Ms. Xu, is twenty-six years old this year. They have only one daughter, named Da Meizi, who is only six years old. She is petite and intelligent, and her parents cherish her dearly. Yesterday morning at eleven o'clock, Ms. Xu sent her daughter out to fetch water. Fang Pei, residing at No. 58 Dao Chong Guan Street, who is sixteen years old, saw Meizi's innocence and purity, and his animalistic desires were aroused. He dragged the girl to a nearby toilet and forcibly violated her. The girl, being young, was unable to resist and was subjected to his actions. Afterwards, her lower body was bruised and swollen, and her pants were stained with blood. The girl limped home and tearfully told her mother what happened. Ms. Xu was furious upon hearing the news and immediately apprehended Fang, taking him and her daughter to the Second Branch Fourth Precinct of the Public Security Bureau. Patrol Officer Ma Xingzhai briefly questioned them and prepared a document instructing the police to transfer them to the Second Branch for further investigation and prosecution by the court.

▲ Jiangsu Province Prepares to Levy Labor for River Dredging. The Construction Department of Jiangsu Province is actively planning and implementing the levy of labor for river dredging in sixty-one counties, sparing no effort. The proposed regulations for levying labor for river dredging, implementation rules, and organizational regulations for the provincial and county river dredging committees have been successively approved by the Provincial Government Committee. The river dredging regulations had already been issued to the counties for compliance. The department will soon issue the river dredging implementation rules, organizational regulations for the county river dredging committees, simplified surveying and design methods, a standard table of surveying expenses, and river survey forms, instructing the county magistrates to supervise and implement them in conjunction with the Construction Bureau.

▲ Exemption from Outstanding House Rent Tax. The Nantong County Government, upon receiving a provincial order to collect house rent tax for two months, had collected over 17,000 yuan as of recently. The households that had not paid were all poor people. The county government petitioned the Department of Finance to exempt them from collection. They have now received instructions to supplement and submit a table of the overall house rent collection situation for review and decision.

Rugao

▲ Many Die After Eating Whale Meat. On the twenty-third, a huge whale, about thirty feet long and over ten feet in girth, was suddenly discovered on the sandbar of Donghai Beach in Juegang. It was about to die of dehydration. More than ten fishermen from Dongxia near the sandbar agreed to bring knives to cut up the meat for cooking. When the fishermen were butchering the whale, tears suddenly streamed from the whale's eyes. The fishermen did not care and cut off hundreds of pounds of fresh meat, which they cooked and ate with relish. Seventeen people ate the meat together. Unexpectedly, all seventeen of them soon began vomiting and diarrhea, resembling a plague. Despite medical treatment, they died one after another. At the same time, several people who had not eaten the meat also contracted the disease and died because they helped cut the meat. The incident caused a sensation far and wide and is considered miraculous.

Taixian

▲ Actively Promoting the New System of Weights and Measures. Regarding the promotion of the new system of weights and measures in this county, the county government has issued a proclamation notifying all stores manufacturing weights and measures to register within the prescribed time. However, after many days, only a few have complied, while most in the rural areas and those who manufacture door-to-door have not yet complied. To urgently achieve implementation, the county government has specifically ordered the Public Security Bureaus and directly subordinate police stations in each district to conduct strict investigations. If any weights and measures stores are found that have not completed registration procedures, they should be closed down immediately. Those who manufacture door-to-door should also be banned.

The bureau's staff used to be only 170 people. After Li's tenure, more than 100 people were abused, costing a huge amount of public funds. Four methods were also discussed and decided: those who have been appointed but have not yet taken office will not be paid; those who have taken office but have not yet set a salary will be given a salary; those who have taken office for less than one month will be given the salary for this month; those who have been in office for more than one month will be given a resignation salary for one month in addition to this month's salary, but only for those who are in the bureau.

General Manager Liu issued a notice of dismissal, saying that the bureau has a large number of people in the takeover volume, which is really redundant. Tseng Chung-ming

Discussing the Allocation and Loan of the British Boxer Indemnity for Road Construction

The Disposal Status of the Accumulated Portion

The Plan for the Portion That Will Become Due Has Also Been Determined.

According to the Central News Agency, the public is largely unaware of the details of the British Boxer Indemnity issue. A Central News Agency reporter took advantage of Tseng Chung-ming's visit to Shanghai on the train yesterday to conduct an interview and inquire in detail. According to Mr. Tseng, the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity was resolved in the 19th year of the Republic, and the exchange of notes stipulated four principles of application, mainly to serve as China's educational and cultural fund, which could be borrowed for reorganizing and constructing China's railways and for undertaking other productive enterprises. The Third Plenary Session of the Second Central Committee, considering the increasing number of refunded Boxer Indemnities from various countries, resolved that two-thirds would be used for railway expenses and one-third for water conservancy and electrical expenses. The Ministry has used this as the basis for the Indemnity it should receive. The total amount of the British Boxer Indemnity refund is approximately £11,186,500. The Ministry should receive two-thirds, or £7,450,000. From December 1922 to February of this year, the Ministry has received approximately £2,130,000, the two-thirds share of the London Boxer Indemnity. Of this, £1,210,000 has already been allocated for various railways. The remaining £920,000 has also been designated for the Tongxi, Xiang'e, Guangshao, and Zhushao Railways. Furthermore, from March of last year to February of this year, the Ministry should receive over 1,056,000 yuan, and over 1,430,000 yuan has already been loaned out, leaving only over 120,000 yuan. This is the disposal status of the accumulated portion of the British Boxer Indemnity received by the Ministry. As for the portion that will become due, the Ministry has also formulated a distribution plan. From March 1933 to December 1936, the domestic and foreign Indemnity due will be approximately £1,520,000, which is planned to be directly allocated for the Zhushao section of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. From January 1937 to December 1946, the domestic Indemnity due will be approximately £1,600,000, which is planned to be used as a fund to issue £1,200,000 in public bonds, with the actual proceeds given to the Zhushao section to cover domestic construction costs. From January 1937 to December 1946, the London Indemnity due will be approximately £1,600,000, which is planned to be used as a fund to issue £1,200,000 in public bonds, with the actual proceeds retained by the Zhushao section for material purchases. This proposed loan allocation of the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity to serve as a fund for issuing Guangdong-Hankou Railway public bonds has been approved by the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees, and the Ministry has drafted a plan and submitted it for review, including fifteen detailed measures, using the entire Guangdong-Hankou Railway as collateral, with the Ministry assuming full responsibility. The Sino-British Boxer Indemnity Board of Trustees will hold a preparatory meeting on the 3rd of next month and a formal meeting on the 5th. This loan proposal will be formally approved by the board. As for the issue of completing the Guangdong-Hankou Railway, only the Zhuzhou to Lechang section remains unbuilt. The engineering costs for this section are 27,500,000 yuan, equivalent to approximately £1,617,000, and the material costs are £2,145,000, for a total of £3,762,000. The Zhuzhou to Lechang section will be completed over four years, starting next year. In addition to allocating the Ministry's due Indemnity and paying interest, the shortfall in engineering and material costs will amount to a total of £2,376,863. This shortfall will be covered by future public bond issues. As for the Guangshao section, the remaining engineering and material costs, as well as debt repayment, amount to a total of 1,500,000 yuan. Aside from the borrowed Indemnity of 700,000 yuan, an additional 800,000 yuan is still needed. It is planned to order the Guangshao Railway to provide assistance in installments, with the goal of completing the railway for traffic in the shortest possible time.

The preparatory meeting was convened at Moore Memorial Church the night before last. Over twenty people attended, including Yin Zhiling, Yao Shoukang, Zhang Fan, Xu Tong, and others from the China Aviation Construction Association, as well as Wang Gang, Leng Xueqiao, Xu Zicheng, Yu Kuiyuan, and others from the Shanghai Boy Scouts Council. It was resolved to convene a team leader meeting within this week, and assign routes, with two teams of five people each. The publicity area includes the International Settlement, the French Concession, and Nanshi. The China Aviation Association also prepared various prizes. In addition to giving each scout an airplane medal, special awards will be given based on their service performance. The officers of the general office were elected on the spot, including Wang Gang as director, Xu Zicheng as deputy director, and Leng Xueqiao as head of the organizing department, among ten others elected. It is now heard that the planning for this program is proceeding very actively. It is expected that after this publicity campaign, the Shanghai public's understanding of aviation will be clearer, and if it is extended to the whole country in the future, the whole country will know the importance of aviation to save the country.

The County Police Commence Winter Defense

Strict County Magistrate Yan of Shanghai County, considering that thieves are more likely to emerge during the winter season, has personally instructed Yao, the head of the Public Security Section, to pay attention to the local winter defense efforts. The section has drafted a plan and notified all public security sub-bureaus to comply. County Magistrate Yan convened the heads of the sub-bureaus to the county government to personally instruct them on the winter defense measures, ensuring that thieves are eradicated and local security is maintained.

Planning to Dredge the Pu Zhao River Waterway

Requiring an Expenditure of 25,000 Taels

The French Concession Assumes Half

Regarding the dredging of the Pu Zhao River waterway in the city, the Bureau of Public Works, upon receiving instructions from the Municipal Government, immediately began drafting a plan, which was submitted to the Municipal Government yesterday. The plan is for preliminary engineering and requires an expenditure of 25,000 taels. The entire project is under the leadership of the Bureau of Public Works, and since the river also flows around the French Concession, the French Concession authorities will also assume half of the expenditure. After receiving the report, the Municipal Government, on one hand, instructed the Bureau of Finance to allocate the funds, and on the other hand, sent a letter to the French Concession Municipal Council to allocate the funds accordingly. Once the funds are collected, the project can commence.

The Last Mediation of the Chinese Merchant Electric Company Labor Strike is Still Ineffective Yesterday

Labor and Management Will Try to Reconcile Again

If Still Ineffective Tomorrow Evening, It Will Be Submitted to Arbitration

Regarding the labor dispute at the Chinese Merchant Electric Company, the Social Affairs Bureau convened a labor-management mediation committee at 2 PM yesterday for a final mediation. The committee members present included Hu Yida and Chuan Chongde from the labor side, Gu Xinyi and Zhang Xiaoliang from the management side, Jin Zhongjian from the Public Security Bureau, Zhou Lianze from the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Wang Gang, the chairman of the committee, from the Social Affairs Bureau. Zhu Xuefan and Li Yongxiang from the General Labor Union, and Lu Bohong, the company manager, and Tan Honglin and Zhang Zhendong, the leaders of the labor union, were present as observers. First, both sides made statements, and then the discussion began, focusing on: 1. The Across-the-Board Wage Increase. The labor side insisted on an increase of 7 yuan for those earning over 40 yuan and 8 yuan for those earning below 40 yuan. The management side initially agreed to an increase of 2 yuan for those earning below 40 yuan, then agreed to 1 yuan for those earning over 40 yuan, and finally agreed to a uniform increase of 2 yuan. 2. The Allowance for Apprentices Entering the Company. The management side stated that it would establish apprentice treatment regulations and announce them in the shortest possible time. The labor side believed that the announced regulations would disappoint the workers and demanded immediate mediation. 3. The Company's Year-End Bonus Over the Years. The labor side demanded two months' pay for those who had worked for more than one year and one month's pay for those who had worked for less than one year, with the same treatment for those who resigned or were dismissed, and the same treatment for apprentices. The management side insisted on following the established practice. 4. The Pension for Staff, Retirement Fund, and Worker's Welfare and Education Fund should be combined, averaged, and distributed fairly. The management side agreed to consider and announce detailed measures. The labor side demanded immediate announcement. The chairman of the committee announced that, since the first and third items could not be mediated, they would be submitted to the Municipal Government for arbitration in accordance with the Labor Dispute Resolution Law. For the second and fourth items, after the management side announces the detailed measures, if the labor side is dissatisfied, mediation will be conducted again in accordance with the law. The labor side demanded that all four conditions be handled together, but the chairman's repeated exhortations were ineffective. The chairman then announced that the labor and management sides would try to reconcile again. If reconciliation is possible, both sides will jointly report to the competent authorities to close the case. If no resolution is reached by 5 PM on the 30th, it will be submitted to the Municipal Government for arbitration. They dispersed around 10 PM.

Local News 2

Accountant Jiang Wanping Convenes

Meeting of Creditors of Yang Qinghe Jewelry Store

Liquidator Proposes That Creditors Participate in the Handling

Yang Qinghe Jiuji Jewelry Store on Nanjing Road, due to financial difficulties, announced its liquidation on the 27th of last month, and entrusted accountant Jiang Wanping and lawyer Jiang Yiping to handle the liquidation matters on its behalf. Yesterday, the case's agents, accountant Jiang and lawyer Jiang, convened a meeting of creditors at the Ningbo Native Place Association on Xizang Road. Accountant Jiang's audit of the jewelry store's asset-liability summary table and related schedules, totaling twelve volumes, were displayed for creditors to review. Chen Longtian and Dong Chunbiao, two accounting assistants from Jiang Wanping's accounting firm, along with all the staff, were present to assist and welcome attendees. About one hundred creditors attended, and lawyers representing the creditors, including Zhang Shizhao, Chen Zemin, Jiang Baoli, Zhou Shaoqin, and Sun Dequan, were also present. First, accountant Jiang announced the purpose of the meeting, stating briefly that liquidation cases involve hundreds of people, and those directly involved are even more numerous. We should pay close attention to such cases with the principle of serving society as our main goal. Observing recent social situations, whenever liquidation cases are announced, all parties involved become overly anxious and panic unnecessarily. We should thoroughly clarify the internal situation and handling standards early to reassure the creditors. However, due to the meticulous procedures of inspecting assets and liabilities, no report can be made until completion. Therefore, the creditors' meeting is scheduled for this Sunday to report publicly. As agents in liquidation cases, although we are nominally entrusted by the parties concerned, we are actually managing the debtor's existing assets on behalf of the creditors, handling them properly, and impartially safeguarding the common interests of all creditors. Our position, according to law, is as a notary for both parties, not as representatives of one side. We cannot protect any one side. Before today's meeting, I believe that all creditors must be anxious and doubtful. After today's meeting, all creditors will have a thorough understanding of everything and can calm their minds. 2. Accountant Jiang reported on the liquidation progress. 3. Accountant Dong Chunbiao, representing accountant Jiang, reported on the asset-liability situation, with detailed explanations. The secured liabilities totaled 41,653.55 taels, and the unsecured liabilities totaled 365,992.90 taels (foreign debts were converted to silver at the rate of 70% of a tael), for a total debt of 419,870.10 taels. The total value of the existing assets was 562,087.33 taels. After deducting the jewelry store's losses of over 270,000 taels from speculative investments and bad debts and depreciation over the years, the actual assets included over 840 taels of gold and silver goods, over 15,000 taels of silver goods, buildings, business assets, goodwill, and various receivables, totaling approximately 170,000 taels. 4. Lawyer Jiang Yiping reported on the asset disposal methods, stating briefly that the method of valuing and disposing of the assets is very important for creditors. We should solicit public opinions and devise perfect methods. Gold and silver goods are a particularly important part of the existing assets. We should either adopt large-scale discounts for public retail sales, or hand over the original items to banks, or melt them for sale. Please discuss these methods together. We would also like to have several representatives elected by the creditors to jointly handle the gold and silver goods with this lawyer and accountant Jiang so as to make it public and fair. 5. Discussion of Asset Disposal: (A) It was resolved to accept the liquidator's suggestion that five representatives be elected by the creditors to handle the matter jointly with accountant Jiang and lawyer Jiang. The creditor representatives elected were lawyer Zhang Shizhao, lawyer Chen Zemin, Yu Jiaming, Qian Xiangjiu, and Ju Minzai. (B) Buildings. (C) Business assets. (D) Goodwill. It was resolved that B, C, and D would be handled together, and accountant Jiang and lawyer Jiang would expedite negotiations for their sale. 6. The Collection and Prosecution of Debts. It was resolved that accountant Jiang and lawyer Jiang would handle the matter. 7. Dismissal of Employees. It was resolved to resolve the matter quickly according to custom in order to save expenses. 8. Handling of Debts. It was resolved to handle the matter according to law. 9. Discussion of Methods When Assets Are Insufficient to Cover Debts. Accountant Jiang presented the jewelry store's capital book, and it was resolved to handle the matter according to law. The meeting concluded at 1 PM.

Wen Hong'en, the Director of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, recently received a confidential report from the Investigation Section that communist leaders Yang Kaishan, Zhao Xiangzhi, Jiang Zhenguo, Huang Shoushan, and others were holding a meeting of communist cadres at 21 Hengshou Lane, Hengtong Road, Zhabei, yesterday morning, plotting illicit activities. Notorious Robber

Zhou Yiwen Executed by Hanging

The notorious robber Zhou Yiwen (also known as Meng Xiaozhou) from Funing, Jiangbei, was involved in an incident in January of the year before last when he led a gang armed with weapons intending to commit unlawful acts. Chinese Constable No. 875 from the Harbin Police Department noticed their suspicious behavior on Dengtuo Road and approached them for questioning. Zhou opened fire, resisting arrest and killing the constable. As a result, Zhou and several of his accomplices were arrested by the detectives and taken to the Eighth Police Department. It was discovered that Zhou and others had committed nine robberies within the jurisdiction. They were sent to the First Special Court for trial and sentencing. Zhou Yiwen was sentenced to death, and the other robbers were punished accordingly. The sentence was reported to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for approval. Yesterday afternoon, the execution date arrived. At around 2 PM, the police escorted Zhou to the Third Criminal Court of the Special Court, where Judge Shen Shanzeng took the bench and asked Zhou if he had any last words. According to Zhou, he was 34 years old and his original name was Meng Xiaozhou. Since he had no relatives in Shanghai, there was no need for him to write a letter. He looked around as if he was trying to find someone. Judge Shen ordered him sent to the Local Court for verification. Chinese and foreign police officers then took Zhou down, along with the case files and photos, and escorted him onto a car, which drove directly to the Caohejing execution ground. At the same time, the Local Court was notified, and the prosecutor and bailiffs arrived at the scene. As Zhou was convicted of murder, he was executed by hanging. According to regulations, the corpse will be displayed overnight and will be collected for burial today.

Textile Factory

The Bed and Matting Cannot Accommodate Each Other

Resentment Increases Due to Salary Increase

Hu Zhigang Murders with a Knife

Ding Jintang Severely Injured

Attempted Suicide Backfires, Claiming a Life

At approximately 1:40 AM yesterday, a murder occurred at the Shen Hsin No. 1 Textile Factory, located at No. 468 Yangshupu Road. According to reports, the factory employed two *chàng xí* (bed and matting, referring to colleagues) workers, one named Hu Zhigang, 25 years old, and the other named Ding Jintang, 23 years old, both from Wuxi. Although they were colleagues, their personalities clashed, so they rarely interacted. Hu was young and impetuous, often making things difficult for others, especially Ding. However, Ding always ignored him. Hu became even more tyrannical, seeing Ding's concession as a sign of weakness and verbally abused him to his face. Ding still endured it. This spring, the factory increased salaries as usual. Considering that Hu and Ding had the same job responsibilities, the factory decided to pay them the same salary. Hu's original salary was 16 yuan, and he received an increase of 4 yuan. Ding's original salary was 12 yuan, and he received an increase of 8 yuan. Unexpectedly, Hu believed that Ding was cunning and persuaded the factory to treat them differently. As a result, Hu harbored even deeper resentment towards Ding and constantly thought of revenge. However, Ding was unaware of this. At approximately 1:40 AM yesterday, all the factory employees were asleep. Suddenly, Hu Zhigang emerged from his dormitory, Room 212, carrying a sharp knife. He went straight to Ding's dormitory, Room 208, opened the door, and entered. At the time, Ding was sound asleep and did not notice Hu wielding the knife and stabbing him violently. He woke up in pain and realized that Hu had pinned him down, preventing him from moving. He shouted loudly from under the covers, waking up his roommates. They got up and saw Hu standing in front of Ding's bed, holding a sharp knife with a furious expression. Ding was rolling on the side of the bed, calling for help, and the blanket was stained with blood. The roommates immediately took Ding to Shanghai General Hospital for treatment. At the same time, they contacted the security guard to report the incident to the police station after dawn. However, while the employees were in a state of confusion, they suddenly saw blood coming out of Hu's orifices and his face turning pale. They quickly questioned him, and Hu confessed that he had taken an antidepressant before committing the crime. The colleagues, upon learning this, quickly sent Hu to Shanghai East Hospital for treatment. However, the poison had been ingested for too long and had seeped into his bloodstream, making it impossible to save him. The hospital reported the death to the Yulin Road Police Station, who transported the body to the Fei Lun Road morgue. Yesterday morning, the court was requested to conduct an autopsy. It was also learned that Ding's injuries were quite severe, and it was uncertain whether he would survive.

Japanese Merchants in Shanghai

Planning to Establish a Department Store

Taking Advantage of the Relaxation of Chinese Boycott

Implementing a Dumping Policy of Japanese Goods

Preparing for a Scheduled Opening

Japanese goods have been successfully dumped in China, and imports have gradually returned to their pre-September 18th state. The goods stored in Shanghai warehouses have been gradually cleared. Japanese merchants are taking it a step further by planning to establish a Japanese department store in Shanghai, specializing in the sale of Japanese products, as a fundamental policy to maximize the distribution of inferior goods. Preparations have been completed, and the details are as follows:

A Northern Fortune Company, orchestrated by Japanese merchants, has a great commercial influence in Shanghai. Before the January 28th Incident, it established the Shishan Glass Factory, the Northern Fortune Soda Factory, and so on. During the war, it had to suspend operations because it was within the line of fire. Now that Japanese merchants in Shanghai are gradually resuming business, the Northern Fortune Company is also planning to resume operations. Recently, it was orchestrated by Yokotake, a Japanese commercial official stationed in Shanghai. To facilitate the sales of Japanese goods, he discussed with Northern Fortune Company the establishment of a large department store in Shanghai, raising one million yuan, specializing in the sale of goods produced throughout Japan. Yokotake has already contacted factories in Japan to arrange for the goods to be shipped to Shanghai as soon as possible.

The location for this large department store has been determined by Northern Fortune Company, Yokotake, and others at the corner of Miller Road and Minhang Road. It will be named the Northern Fortune Department Store, specializing in the sale of Japanese products. Goods from other countries will not be sold, as its aim is to take advantage of the waning Chinese boycott movement to develop outlets for Japanese goods. It also aims to sell at low prices and has set the official opening date for December 15th. Currently, they are arranging the store and stocking the shelves.

The store will be very large and comprehensive, with a wide variety of goods, including grains, Western-style pastries, seafood, ceramics, enamelware, woolen textiles, cotton textiles, hemp products, clothing, toys, leather goods, stationery, medicines, tobacco and alcohol, metal products, jewelry, and various other items. Even products from Hokkaido will be transported to Shanghai for sale.

Yangtze River Navigation Facilities

To Continue to be Managed by Customs

The jurisdiction over navigation facilities along the Yangtze River, such as lighthouses and buoys, which was disputed by the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Transportation, has now been reviewed by the Central Political Conference. It was unanimously agreed that these navigation facilities are related to national tax revenue and navigation convenience and have been managed by the Customs for a long time, with a well-established system and outstanding results. Therefore, the Customs should continue to manage them. The Executive Yuan of the National Government has been ordered to comply. The Shanghai General Tax Office has also received the instruction.

Road Extension Dispute

Transformed into a Dispute between Britain and Japan

Over the Issue of Appointing a Japanese Deputy Police Chief versus a British One

The British Side Considers the Municipal Council as a Whole Organization

The road extension issue in the Shanghai International Settlement has been stalled due to Japanese opposition. There is still no new progress on the matter. However, according to information obtained by a reporter from the *Xinsheng She* (New Sound News Agency) yesterday, the case has already evolved from a dispute between the Municipal Council and the Japanese side into a dispute between Britain and Japan. According to a Japanese official spokesperson speaking to the reporter, the case is currently being negotiated among the Japanese Consul Ishiya, the British Consul Brenan, and the Director-General of the Municipal Council, Fessenden, but there has been no significant progress. The spokesperson stated that what the Japanese side is demanding is the issue of the Deputy Police Chief. The agreement stipulates that the Police Chief should be Chinese and the Deputy Police Chief should be British. The Japanese side insists that a Japanese national should be appointed as Deputy Police Chief based on the proportion of the number of Japanese residents in Shanghai, the number of British residents in Shanghai, and the qualifications for paying taxes. The spokesperson did not mention whether the Japanese government had any new instructions but said that the Japanese side attaches great importance to this point. If this point is resolved, then everything else will not be a problem, and the signing can be implemented immediately. The British side's attitude is that the Municipal Council is a whole organization, without distinguishing between the number of Japanese residents and the number of British residents.

Postponement of Japanese Military Withdrawal

The commander of the Japanese Navy Third Fleet, Sakonji, returned to Japan on the *Izumo* warship on the afternoon of the 27th. The 300 Japanese sailors and 150 marines who were scheduled to withdraw from Shanghai were originally scheduled to leave Shanghai on the *Qingdao* transport ship at the same time as the *Izumo*. However, due to insufficient time to board the ship, the departure was postponed to the 30th of this month. Furthermore, the Japanese military police who were to be repatriated to Japan left Shanghai at 9:00 AM yesterday, led by Major Obata with 80 soldiers, aboard the *Shanghai Maru*. The remaining base and troops are scheduled to return to Japan in early December.

Delay in Signing Cross-Border Telephone Agreement

Regarding the cross-border road and telephone agreement in the Public Concession, after it was approved by the Municipal Council, our City Public Utilities Bureau and the South City Telephone Bureau also received orders from the Central Government and the Ministry of Transportation to proceed with the signing procedures with the Public Concession Telephone Company. Both parties originally planned to formally sign the agreement today or tomorrow. Yesterday, it was learned that the company must obtain written permission from the Municipal Council before it can be implemented. Currently, both parties are comparing and organizing the text. After the organization is completed, the Telephone Company will submit it to the Municipal Council for review. After receiving a reply, the signing can be implemented. It is unlikely to be realized this week and will be postponed to next week.

*Song Bao* Continues Publication in Shanghai

Yesterday's Letter to the County Government Declares Intention

After being forced to cease publication, the composing room of *Songjiang Song Bao* was also monitored by police sent by the authorities, making printing impossible. Yesterday, the paper moved to No. 278 Huile Lane, Yunnan Road, Shanghai, to continue editing and publishing. At the same time, a letter was sent directly to the Songjiang County Government Public Security Bureau declaring its intention to resume publication, in order to comply with procedures. The newspaper's official letter is excerpted as follows: "Respectfully, at 10:00 PM on the 22nd of this month, Chen Shuliang, Inspector-General of the Public Security Bureau, and Jiang Xiawu, patrol officer of the Second Sub-Station, ordered our newspaper to cease publication and sent police to monitor the composing room, prohibit mailing, and arrest newspaper employees. As for the reasons for ordering the cessation of publication, the officials stated that they were acting on a confidential order from your government. Under this authority, our newspaper, unable to withstand the pressure, ceased publication on the 23rd, awaiting further instructions from your government. However, after waiting until now, no signs have emerged. The public is suspicious and unable to fathom the depth of the situation. However, given this extra-legal destruction, our newspaper finds it difficult to remain silent. After consideration by our colleagues, rather than suffering extra-legal sanctions and inviting criticism from the world, it is better to continue publication to demonstrate the spirit of the rule of law. Therefore, in addition to continuing publication and reporting to our superiors, we are sending this letter for your information."

Fire in the French Concession This Morning

Fire at Tianfu Store

Spreads to Several Neighbors

At 0:15 AM this morning, a fire suddenly broke out on the ground floor of the Tianfu Run Department Store at No. 8, the intersection of Jixiang Street and Sanyangjing Bridge in the French Concession. At the time, the neighbors and the store's employees were already asleep, so they did not notice the fire until it reached the stairs, waking them from their dreams. At the same time, the neighbors were also awakened and fled in panic. Before long, flames erupted through the roof. The nearby police reported to the French Concession Fire Brigade, which quickly dispatched fire engines to the scene to put out the fire. However, the wind was strong, and the fire spread rapidly with the wind, engulfing the neighboring houses. Nos. 6 Fuxinglong Leather Suitcase Store, 10 Dongwanyu General Merchandise Store, 12 Zhou Shunjiyang Iron Store, and 14 Zhou Shunxiang Department Store were all affected. The situation quickly became uncontrollable. Fire engines from various sections also rushed to help put out the fire. When the reporter returned to the office after the investigation, the fire had not yet subsided. The flames were spreading directly into the Deqing Lane in that area. The firefighters were working hard to put out the fire, hoping to prevent it from spreading further.

Northeast Naval Shipyard Construction

Qingdao Mayor and Navy Commander Shen Honglie has repeatedly telegraphed Tao Guilin, General Manager of Fook Kee Construction, to discuss plans and engineering for the construction of a naval factory shipyard. Tao will take a ship north on the 15th of this month to meet with Mayor Shen to discuss the project. The shipyard is planned to be 500 feet long, based on the *Haiqi* warship as a standard. It is one of the most important shipyards in Beiyang. If the construction is successful, it will have a close relationship with industry, transportation, and ship repair. Mayor Shen has entrusted all the engineering to Fook Kee Construction and signed a contract at the Qingdao Naval Headquarters on the 22nd of this month. Tao returned to Shanghai yesterday to prepare for the project.

Changxing Launches

Chinese Philippine Islands Travel Group

Round Trip in Twelve Days

Only £22 Needed

Chinese citizens traveling to the Philippines usually require entry passports, and the procedures are unusually complicated. Now, the Changxing Steamship Company of this city is launching a Chinese travel group to the Philippine Islands during the Christmas season. It has obtained the consent of the Governor-General of the Philippines to waive passport requirements. The company has scheduled the Asian Queen to leave Shanghai on December 20th for a 12-day trip. Passengers can disembark and tour Hong Kong for four days, visit the Philippine Islands for three days, and then return to Shanghai. The round-trip travel cost is only £22, which is only about half the regular fare.

Page 12

Building Association

Diligent Study of Architectural Science

The Shanghai Architectural Association is a group of the Shanghai architectural community. Its purpose is to study academics and improve the architectural industry. In addition to compiling and publishing the Architectural Monthly, which contains specialized disciplines of architectural construction and structural drawings, the association has organized an architectural academic discussion meeting to seek concrete improvements. It widely solicits those with rich knowledge and experience in architecture to join the discussion, in order to gather ideas and achieve great results. People such as Mr. Shen Yi, Yang Ximou, Zhao Shen, Zhuang Jun, Zhang Xiaoliang, Qian Shaoping, Li Keng, Li Mengbo, Dong Dayou, Tang Jingxian, Ben Yan Geng, etc., are all on the invitation list. Their future achievements will be extremely impressive. The first step of the association's discussion is to determine the names of architectural technologies and materials. The architecture in various parts of our country is complex and inconsistent. Moreover, architectural materials from Europe and the United States have new products every day. Our country initially had no fixed names and called them by their original names. As new products increase, difficult and obscure names become even more mixed, which is indeed an obstacle to the future of the architectural industry. The association, in view of this, plans to discuss it as soon as possible. After a definite name is decided, it will be announced to the national architectural community for unified adoption in order to unify and facilitate improvement.

Wu Shaoda's Reactionary Suspicion, Declared Not Guilty After Retrial

Wu Shaoda from Shaoxing was arrested last year in the French Concession by Chinese and foreign detectives of the French Police Political Department on suspicion of participating in the Communist Party's reactionary activities. He was sent to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court and prosecuted for endangering the Republic of China. Wu hired lawyers Wang Shizong and others to defend him. He was sentenced to two years and six months of imprisonment. Wu refused to accept the judgment and filed an appeal to the Supreme Court, which was sent back for retrial. The Third Branch of the Higher Court received the case file. Because this case was a special case, the Party Department dispatched members to the court to participate in the jury according to regulations. Therefore, it notified the Shanghai Municipal Party Department to send Chen Zhigao, Huang E, Zhang Jiaodao, Jiang Huaisu, Wang Deyan, Wu Zhengjue and other six members to the court. It also informed the police department's lawyer. Presiding Judge Zhou Yunhui, together with judges Guo Dezhang and Zhao Zhenhai, and Chief Prosecutor Zhao Shibei, together with the jurors, specially opened the First Criminal Court and ordered the police to bring the appellant Wu Shaoda for retrial. The appellant was still defended by lawyers Wang Shizong and Yu Zhongluo. As a result, the debate was declared over. Yesterday, Wu Shaoda was declared not guilty. Subsequently, Wu was released on bail by the owner of Shusanhe Foil Shop in Ximennei Chuanqinhe.

Taicang Escapee Sentenced

Five robbers, Sheng Yunsheng, Zheng Shanghe, Li Guodong, Gao Yunshan, and Xu Shouzheng (all escapees who committed crimes and were imprisoned in Taicang on March 3rd of this year), came to Shanghai. They colluded with Zou Zhongxi and Chen Chunhe, and robbed six households, including Chen Anquan at 54 Dongxi Huade Road and Chen Wangshi at 103 Xinji浜 Road, of clothing and silver dollars worth more than 1,500 yuan. After the case was discovered and they escaped, they were arrested by Chinese and foreign detectives of the Huishan Police Department and sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation and final sentencing. This has been reported in this newspaper. The day before yesterday, Judge Zhao Linxuan presided over the Third Criminal Court and sentenced Sheng Yunsheng and Zheng Shanghe to ten years of imprisonment each, Zou Zhongxi to eight years of imprisonment, Xu Shouzheng to seven years of imprisonment, Chen Chunhe to four years of imprisonment, Gao Yunshan to one year and six months of imprisonment, and Li Guodong to one year of imprisonment. The number of days of detention before the judgment is final will be converted to one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention.
