Chen Atang's Tomb Enclosed in Public Cemetery

According to Guowen News Agency, the case of Chen Atang, a Puxi resident who was beaten to death by a Japanese sailor some years ago, was negotiated with the Japanese side for a long time with the assistance of lawyer Wu Kaisheng and various united groups. As a result, two Japanese sailors were sentenced by the Nagasaki Local Court to two years of imprisonment and two years of detention each, for a total of four years. At the same time, the person in charge of the Japanese side contributed 3,000 yuan as compensation for Chen Atang's family to handle the aftermath. Subsequently, Chen's wife, Ms. Song, purchased more than one mu of land in Jinjiahang, Puxi Twenty-one Tu, and filled in the graves of Chen Atang's ancestors and grandparents, a total of six graves, and buried them in that place. It has been five years. Unexpectedly, in June of this year, someone initiated the organization of the Pudong Jiu'an Cemetery in that area, enclosing 60 mu of land, all purchased from the villagers at public prices. The tomb base of Atang and others was also enclosed, and the selling price was collected by Chen Yunmei, Atang's uncle. When Chen's wife, Ms. Song, heard this news, she was greatly alarmed and invited many representatives from all walks of life to go to Pudong to negotiate with the Jiu'an Cemetery office and Chen Yunmei. As a result, Chen Yunmei wrote a guarantee, stating that after the cemetery is completed, the six graves of Atang and others will still be buried in it in the Jiu'an style. He also entrusted lawyer Wu Kaisheng to request protection and transferred a letter to inform him.

Jiangwan District Tenants' Association Inaugural Meeting

Since the January 28th Incident, industries and businesses in Jiangwan have been completely devastated, and the losses are incalculable. The financial resources of the people have been trapped in a difficult situation after this catastrophe. Unexpectedly, a small number of landlords in the district have greatly increased rents and added transfer fees, hoping to increase their income, causing the tenants in the area to suffer greatly. They had no choice but to initiate a tenants' union. After a month of preparation, the inaugural meeting was held at 1:00 PM on November 27th in the auditorium of the Seventh District Party Department. More than 100 tenants attended. Li Xiamin was elected as chairman. The meeting was held as scheduled. The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting and the preparations. Representatives gave speeches in succession and discussed five proposals: ㈠ Pass the constitution, ㈡ Reduce rent by half, ㈢ The transfer fee should be based on the amount of three months' rent, ㈣ Rent donations should be temporarily exempted until the original state is restored, ㈣ The rent due this month will be paid painfully while waiting for a solution, ㈤ Elect Li Yannong, Li Xiamin, Yin Zixi, Ding Boqi, Wang Tingtao, Zhou Bodong, and Jiang Peigen as executive committee members, Lu Tonghou and Cao Yushu as alternates, and Zhao Genxiang, Xuan Fuqing, and Tan Juchang as supervisory committee members, and Jiang Muliang and Lu Guixiang as alternate committee members.

Shi Wanqing, a 52-year-old Jiangbei resident, was a foreman at the Public Works Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council. Yesterday, he was suddenly hit by tram number 1375 on Yangshupu Road, and his head was severely crushed. Afterwards, the police arrived and sent him to the Sacred Heart Hospital by car. He died shortly after treatment. Recent Events in the Medical and Pharmaceutical Circles

Specialized Gynecology Hospital There are many hospitals in Shanghai, but there is no specialized gynecology hospital established by Chinese people. Women feel inconvenient to seek treatment when they are sick. Dr. Gu Zongnv has established Shude Hospital in Shanghai for many years and has saved countless lives. In response to the needs of the times, a specialized gynecology hospital has been established at the intersection of Xixinqiao Ningbo Road in the French Concession. It is large in scale and fully equipped, with many internal wards for patients to be hospitalized for treatment. Two female doctors are also hired to assist in the diagnosis. Dr. Zhu Daozhou, the former director of surgery at the Union Hospital, is also hired as a special physician. The clinic will open on the 29th of this month.

China-Switzerland Hospital Mr. Niao Pinrui, a giant in the woolen industry, in view of the fact that there are still few eye, ear, nose, and throat hospitals established in Shanghai, and there are many people suffering from eye, ear, nose, and throat diseases, specially ordered his son, Mr. Jia Lun, to jointly fund and organize the China-Switzerland Eye, Ear, Nose, and Throat Specialist Hospital with Swiss people residing in Shanghai. The hospital site has now been surveyed and determined to be at 618 Nanjing Road (upstairs in the Ruotai Woolen Store). The internal equipment is extremely complete, and Professor Gaolang, a Swiss doctor and director of the Department of Ophthalmology, Otolaryngology and Head and Neck Surgery at Aurora University Medical College and Guangci Hospital, is hired as the director of medical affairs, and Dr. Qiling is the deputy director. In order to benefit the common people and start treatment, outpatient clinics are open from 10:00 AM to 12:00 PM, and the consultation fee is only six corners, in order to widely distribute benevolence. It is also heard that the hospital is scheduled to officially open on the 11th of this month.

He is unwilling to keep it secret, and publishes the prescription to help the world, and supervises the production himself. Those who suffer from this disease in various ports who buy and take it all recover completely, so letters of thanks must be received several times a day. This pill not only has the effect of removing lao, but also is a holy product for cultivating and replenishing Zhenyuan. Each material is four boxes of ocean Nian Yuan, and each box is four yuan. Letters to the Editor

To the Editor, This newspaper reported today that the Huaxingchang Machinery Factory on Maohai Road was searched and found 45 fake guns and 47 bayonets. According to the person in charge of the factory, the fake guns were custom-made by the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce School. Because the style was different from the original design, they were unwilling to ship the goods and were left in the factory. After investigation, the night school run by our association aims to study practical business academics. There is no subject of military gymnastics in the curriculum, so there is no custom-made fake guns and equipment from outside. I am deeply afraid that the factory's misinformation will cause suspicion from the outside world. I am writing to inform you and respectfully hope that your newspaper will publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column to make a statement. This is to the Shen Bao Newspaper. Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, November 28.

To the Editor, For the sake of declaring injustice, suffering unbearable pain, and requesting (the 18th of this month) to correct your newspaper, so as to clarify right and wrong and avoid innocent suffering, my son, Zhu Adong, lives on the third floor of 162 Manchuria Road, Zhabei. The family of five makes a living by hiring workers. Unfortunately, at 4 AM on the 17th of this month, a fire broke out in the middle floor. The ladder had been broken, and there was no way to escape. Then the 14-year-old young daughter died in the fire. Those who were able to escape were all seriously injured. Then, the old man's head was severely injured and his life was uncertain. At that time, the police officers did not understand the correct situation and immediately detained the young man Zhu Adong and sent him to the court, according to what was published in your newspaper, to punish the person who caused the fire. The second floor where the fire actually started was empty, and in addition to being able to obtain special new fire insurance fees, they can enjoy themselves outside the law. Is this unfair? At present, various places have already understood the true situation that the ladder on the second floor was burned off and the 14-year-old young daughter could not escape, and she was burned to death in the fire. The truth can be investigated and verified. For this reason, I am writing to request a swift correction, based on the facts, according to justice, to prove that it was not the young man Zhu Adong who caused the fire, and according to the fact that the ladder on the second floor was burned off, it is a definite proof that the fire started, so as to avoid the young man Zhu Adong suffering innocently, and according to the fairness and impartiality of your newspaper, I respectfully submit this to the Editor of the Shen Bao Newspaper for consideration. Zhu Zhang Shi Jinzhen, November 27, 21st year.

Director Weng Arrived in Beijing but Did Not Take Office

His Mother is Critically Ill, He Returned to Beiping Yesterday

Nanjing, 28th Telegram The Ministry of Education announced on the 28th that Director Weng arrived in Beijing on the 26th and originally planned to go to the Ministry to take up the war within days. On the evening of the 27th, he suddenly received a telegram from Beiping, saying that his mother was critically ill with a stroke and only wanted him to return quickly. On the evening of the 28th, he took the Pingpu train north. Director Weng did not go to the Ministry on the morning of the 28th to take over the job and return to Beiping. He did not express when he would come to Beijing to take over the job again. After arriving in Beijing, Weng's whereabouts were secret and he never saw guests. Minister Jian Changzhao also denied that Weng lived in his residence. On the 28th, the Ministry of Education received four telegrams from Xu Fan, Qia Yan, Fu Qingli, Li Shutian, and the Belgian Student Association congratulating Weng on his appointment, but Weng did not go to the Ministry and could not deliver them. Chemical and Pharmaceutical Terminology

Nanjing, 28th Telegram The Compilation and Translation Bureau submitted to the Ministry of Education a request to announce chemical nomenclature and pharmaceutical terms. The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 28th to change chemical nomenclature to chemical nomenclature principles and announce them together with pharmaceutical terms. This chemical nomenclature principle is divided into four parts: one part for naming principles, two for elements, three for inorganic compounds, and four for organic compounds. Pharmaceutical terms will divide each term into Latin name, German name, English name, Japanese name, chemical or decided name preparation, and other columns, and list the translations of chemical and pharmaceutical names in detail.

Anhui Provincial No. 3 Girls' Middle School is located in Fengyang. The principal was changed this summer. There was student unrest at the time of the handover, which has now been calmed down. Issued by the Ministry of Education

Kindergarten and Elementary School Curriculum Standards (9)

Attachment 1: Explanation of Various Literary Styles

(A) General Prose

(1) Narrative Writing: (i) Life Stories: stories that narrate real life with children's perspectives as the main focus; (ii) Nature Stories: stories about the lives and characteristics of natural objects (stories of scientific inventions also fall into this category); (iii) Historical Stories: stories that relate historical facts about people or events (biographical anecdotes and personal achievements of inventors also fall into this category); (iv) Fairy Tales: supernatural hypothetical stories; (v) Legends: folk tales, including primitive stories; (vi) Fables: short stories containing moral significance; (vii) Jokes: short, humorous, and laughable stories; (viii) Diaries; (ix) Travelogues; (x) Other. (2) Expository Writing; (3) Essays. (B) Practical Writing

(1) Letters: correspondence between people or between personified objects (such as magpies and swallows); (2) Notices: announcements and advertisements of schools or children's self-governing bodies; (3) Other.

(C) Poetry and Songs

(1) Nursery Rhymes: songs that conform to children's psychology (tongue twisters, etc., also fall into this category); (2) Folk Songs: folk ballads passed down by word of mouth (imitations of folk songs also fall into this category); (3) Miscellaneous Songs: all songs that describe scenery, express emotions, narrate stories, etc. (ballads, lyrics also fall into this category); (4) Riddles: including imitations; (5) Poems: what modern people call new poetry and the vernacular poems of the ancients.

(D) Scripts

(1) Spoken Drama; (2) Opera.

Attachment 2: Allocation of Reading Material Quantity

(A) Regarding Literary Styles

Grade Percentage Category Grades 1-2 Grades 3-4 Grades 5-6

General 70 70 70

Practical 0 10 15

Poetry 3 15 10

Drama 0 5 5

(B) Regarding Content

Grade Percentage Category Grades 1-2 Grades 3-4 Grades 5-6

Civics 30 30 30

Nature 35 20 10

History 0 20 25

Literature 20 10 5

Party Doctrine 10 10 15

Hygiene 5 5 5

Geography 0 5 15

Attachment 3: The Compilation and Selection of Teaching Materials Should

Pay attention to the following points...

(1) Based on the principles of our Party, teaching materials should be as rich as possible in the spirit of sacrifice and mutual assistance. All teaching materials containing selfishness, self-interest, usurpation, competition, Qing Dynasty nostalgia, backwardness, Eastern restraints, escapist ideology, aristocratic tendencies, capitalist tendencies, etc., should be avoided. Teaching materials on Party doctrine that are critical and left-leaning should be actively adopted. (i) When considering stories of Mr. Sun Yat-sen: (A) Childhood life; (B) Student life; (C) Revolutionary affairs; (D) Birth and death anniversaries; (E) Other. (ii) Regarding stories and poems about the National Revolution: (A) The national flag and party flag; (B) Various important revolutionary anniversaries (such as the Huanghuagang Uprising, the Wuchang Uprising, etc.); (D) Other. (iii) Regarding stories and poems that inspire national spirit: (A) Facts about patriotism and national revolution; (B) Facts related to the achievements and culture of the Chinese nation; (C) Important days of national humiliation; (D) Regarding the humiliation of our people and overseas Chinese by imperialists; (E) Other. (iv) Regarding stories and poems that inspire the concept of civil rights: (A) Breaking the superstition of divine power; (B) Breaking the belief in military power and the feudal ideology and remnants of feudal forces; (C) Guiding equality, mutual assistance, discipline, etc.; (D) Regarding the civil rights movement; (E) Other. (v) Regarding stories and poems that cultivate the concept of people's livelihood: (A) Labor Day and the agricultural and industrial workers' movement; (B) Regarding afforestation, agricultural improvement, and industrial movement; (C) Regarding promoting domestic goods; (D) Regarding cooperative production and cooperative consumption; (E) Other. (2) Based on the principle of increasing children's reading ability, imaginative teaching materials (such as fables, fairy tales, etc.) and realistic teaching materials (such as nature stories, life stories, historical stories, etc.) should be harmonized and balanced. All teaching materials with a terrifying nature should be avoided as much as possible.

(3) Based on the principle of increasing children's reading interest, teaching materials should be as artistically interesting as possible. The conditions are as follows: (i) The facts are connected consistently and not cluttered; (ii) The interest is deep and enduring, not shallow; (iii) The narration is winding and lively, not dry and rigid; (iv) The wording is sincere and earnest, not superficial and evasive; (v) The description and facts should be "consistent and harmonious," not discordant and incompatible; (vi) Use peculiar arrangements (such as birds and flowers paired together are commonplace; birds paired with songs or speech feel peculiar, making it difficult for children to infer directly); (vii) The structure is tight, complete, not loose and fragmented.

(4) Based on children's psychology, teaching materials should be as relevant to children's lives as possible. The conditions are as follows: (i) Children or characters close to children should be the protagonists in the teaching materials; (ii) Abstract events should be compiled into concrete fragments of facts; (iii) After reading, there should be work to do, things to imagine or research; (iv) More fairy tales, poems, and stories should be used in lower grades; (v) Arrange according to seasons so that teaching is easy to visualize at any time; (vi) The depth of the writing should be appropriate to the children's level.

(5) Based on the principle of using standard language to learn vernacular writing, the organization of words, etc., should be based on standard grammar. The rhyme of poetry, etc., should be based on standard phonetics.

Fourth, Key Teaching Points

(1) Speaking

(i) Start teaching with complete sentences, then use paragraphs of speech. (ii) Teachers should pre-compile cases as language materials. The language materials are divided into three types as follows: (A) Organized and progressive language materials. Each should have a topic, and each sentence should simply describe an action, but not be too complicated (start from one subject and be easy to see and easy to do; there should not be too many sentences in each set); (B) Conversational materials should focus on an interesting event and have an interesting topic; (C) Story language materials should contain children's literary interest and not violate Party doctrine. (iii) Speaking should be natural (not be bound by the nuances of the words), and pay attention to the difference between children's language and adult language. (iv) Speaking should be vivid and have a context. Teaching and actions should be combined with performance. It is best to have children perform the stories that have already been told. (v) Sounds or words that are easily mistaken should be spoken particularly clearly, listened to more, practiced more, and guided to correct them based on the position of pronunciation. Words with unclear meanings should be expressed using real objects, diagrams, actions, explanations, translations, etc.

(2) Reading

(vi) The sequence of material arrangement should pay attention to the following points: (A) Start with progressive and continuous picture stories, then use half-picture and half-text stories. The text of the stories used in grades 3-4 can gradually increase, and the number of pictures can gradually decrease; (B) Use complete story paragraphs to begin text teaching, instead of starting with single words and sentences. After learning the complete story paragraph, recognize sentences from the story, and then recognize words and characters from the sentences. Later, use complete paragraphs or complete articles; (C) Arrange various literary styles in a mixed manner. There should be more poetry in lower grades, and gradually reduce it in upper grades. (vii) Reading teaching should first have a general overview and then a partial analysis, first an absorption of the content and then an exploration of the form, first understanding and then memorization. (viii) The teaching of literary materials should supplement imagination in many ways, and design performances randomly to reveal the content and situation completely, so that children can fully appreciate it. (ix) In addition to intensive reading, there should be regular time to guide children to skim reading. Intensive reading teaching in lower grades emphasizes both reading aloud and silent reading. From the second grade onward, the opportunity for silent reading should be more than that for reading aloud. Teaching reading aloud should pay attention to pronunciation and intonation. Teaching silent reading should pay attention to accuracy, speed, and conciseness (that is, extracting the main points, such as dividing paragraphs and seeking key points). (x) From the second grade onward, opportunities should be taken to briefly point out the meaning of word composition (for example, "smoke" comes from mouth and is burned by fire, and "day" is the sun appearing from the horizon) to help children's memory, and briefly guide simple grammar to enhance children's reading and expression abilities. (xi) The books for skim reading should emphasize appreciation, practicality, and reference, but the proportions vary according to grade. In addition to in-class guidance, children should be encouraged to read outside of class and make reading reports. (xii) Starting from the fourth grade, children should be guided to practice taking reading notes. (3) Writing

(xiii) Whether oral or written, attention should be paid to the value of the content, not just focusing on the form. (xiv) Oral and written descriptions should be closely linked. For example, for the same topic, first give a speech (oral description), then write a description (written description), and then discuss and study it, or first give a speech, then write a description, or first write a description, then discuss it. (xv) In the lower grades, more auxiliary methods can be used for writing guidance; in the middle grades, more imitation methods can be used. (xvi) Develop the habit of making a rough draft. (xvii) The method of setting topics should pay attention to: (i) using opportunities to set topics; (ii) often having children set their own topics; (iii) providing multiple topics for selection. (xviii) The nature of the topics should pay attention to: (i) being relevant to children's lives; (ii) being easy for children to express themselves; (iii) being interesting. (xix) Grading should be serious and should preserve the children's original intentions as much as possible, and give children the opportunity to jointly grade and study. In the upper grades, "correction symbols" can be used to have children revise themselves. (xx) Error correction should be given more guidance. If there are major errors, the grammar and syntax that are prone to error can be fully practiced using imitation and other methods. (xxi) The guidance of syntax and grammar should use an inductive process, based on the materials already taught in the national language, and collect similar materials for comparative study. (xxii) The model for writing should be practical writing with exemplary structure (correct thinking, clear levels, proper format, etc.) and descriptive writing as the main focus. (xxiii) When starting to practice writing, children should be guided to practice diary writing.

(4) Calligraphy

(xxiv) The materials for calligraphy should initially use commonly used characters and easily mistaken characters, and record them as meaningful sentences to reduce rote memorization. (xxv) The posture for calligraphy, the application of tools, and the stroke order, structure, and position of the characters should be carefully guided from the beginning. (xxvi) Pencils should be used for calligraphy at first, for ease of manipulation. In the second grade, in addition to continuing to practice pencil writing, attention should be paid to brush training. In the fifth and sixth grades, brush calligraphy training can be added. (xxvii) Copying (or tracing), head writing (using printed calligraphy models), and free writing (without using models) should be used interchangeably. (xxviii) Regular competitions should be held from time to time.

Anhui Province Investigates and Recovers Education in Bandit Areas

▲ The Education Department Sends Cheng Zun-san and Others to Investigate

The counties of Liu'an, Qushan, Huoqiu, etc., in Anhui Province have been in bandit areas for a long time, and have now been successively recovered. The Education Department specially sent staff member Cheng Zun-san and others to Liu'an, Huoshan, and Huoqiu counties to conduct investigations. The department also formulated twelve measures for reorganizing education in the recovered bandit areas and submitted them to the provincial government for record. The measures include the department sending specialists to the counties to work with the county magistrate and education bureau director to investigate the situation, formulate plans, focus on the screening and ideological correction of teachers, and allow for flexible handling according to local conditions.

Local News

French Concession Private School Federation

Postpones Petition to French Municipal Council

▲ Mayor Wu Has Consulted with the French Consul

▲ The Municipal Education Bureau Convened a Meeting of All Committee Members Yesterday

▲ Ma Jia-zhen's Talk on the Federation's Minimum Demands

The Shanghai French Concession Private Primary and Secondary School Federation originally planned to send all executive and supervisory committee members to the French Municipal Council yesterday to petition for the council to subsidize private schools within the concession with 20% of the total annual income. However, the federation received a notice from the Municipal Education Bureau to postpone the petition and convened a meeting of all executive and supervisory committee members to discuss the matter. After receiving the notice, all supervisory committee members went to the Municipal Education Bureau at 9:00 a.m. yesterday.

▲ The Education Bureau's Opinion Was Received by Yan Fei-cheng, Section Chief of the Bureau, Who Expressed His Views to the Committee Members. He stated that the Bureau fully sympathized with the Federation's request for the French Municipal Council to subsidize private schools and would provide assistance. However, the Bureau believed that the petition could be postponed for the time being. The French Consul had gone to the Municipal Government to consult with Mayor Wu on the matter, and Mayor Wu had sent Secretary Geng of the Municipal Government to the Bureau to dissuade the Federation from petitioning. Yesterday, the Bureau received a letter from Mayor Wu stating that he had contacted the French Consul on the matter and had made some progress. He requested that the petition be postponed for the time being. Therefore, he had convened everyone here today to discuss the matter. The Bureau had decided to work with the Municipal Government to negotiate with the French Municipal Council and would report the results to everyone within a week, hoping to satisfy everyone. The Bureau hoped that the petition would be postponed for the time being. The Japanese believed that the Federation should only request the French Municipal Council to subsidize private schools run by Chinese, and not request the French to establish Chinese schools. The committee members then returned to the federation and decided to postpone the petition to the French Municipal Council and wait for the Municipal Government to resolve the matter.

▲ Ma Jia-zhen's Talk Subsequently, Ma Jia-zhen, a member of the standing committee of the federation, told a Shanghai Social News reporter that since the Municipal Education Bureau and the Municipal Government had agreed to work with the French Municipal Council to negotiate the matter, the federation could wait for a resolution. However, he believed that the French Concession was Chinese territory and that the French Municipal Council could not treat the Chinese in the French Concession as if they were in a colony. The French Municipal Council should seek a balance in the development of education for Westerners and Chinese in the concession. According to a recent survey, the annual education expenditure per Western child was forty-four taels, while the annual education expenditure per Chinese child was only seven mace and two candareens. This disparity was shocking. Therefore, the federation demanded that the French Municipal Council develop Chinese education, and the minimum requirement was that the annual education expenditure per Chinese child should be equal to that of a Western child. He hoped that the Municipal Government and the Municipal Education Bureau would pay attention to this point.

Judging Standards for National Mandarin Recreation Competition

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association has scheduled the first National Mandarin Recreation Competition for the 12th, 13th, and 14th of this month at Shanghai Wanzhu Elementary School. Details have been reported in previous newspapers. It is reported that the association's judging standards are divided into three categories: drama concept, speech, and expression. Drama concept is further divided into two items: thought and structure. Speech is further divided into two items: pronunciation and tone. Expression is further divided into two items: expression and action. The scoring method is based on a percentage system. Drama concept is worth 20 points, with 10 points for each item. Speech is worth 50 points, with 25 points for each item. Expression is worth 30 points, with 15 points for each item. The chairman of the judging panel is the director of the Shanghai Education Bureau. There are six judges, one each month, three of whom are officials from the education sector and three of whom are staff members of the Mandarin Association. During the competition, the judges will score separately, and the rankings will be determined by the total number of points.

Physical Education

Obstacles to Next Year's National Games

The Ministry of Education Has Not Yet Taken Over the Central Stadium

The 20th-Year Preparatory Committee Is Willing to Continue Handling Matters

The organizational regulations and budget for the National Games, scheduled to be held at the Central Stadium in the capital during the Double Tenth Festival next year, have been reviewed and approved by the Executive Yuan meeting on the 15th of this month. At that time, it was also resolved to request the National Government to explicitly abolish the National Games Preparatory Committee of the 20th Year of the Republic and for the Ministry of Education to take over the Central Stadium. These matters have been reported in the newspapers. On the 25th of this month, the standing committee of the Ministry of Education's Education Committee, in response to the failure to establish the preparatory committee for next year's National Games, resolved that "a decision will be made after the Minister of Education consults with Chairman Lin." After investigation, the details have come to light and are summarized as follows: The construction of the Central Stadium was previously managed by the National Games Preparatory Committee of the 20th Year of the Republic. Due to the outbreak of the September 18th Incident, the entire country united against external forces, and the National Games were suspended. However, the National Games Preparatory Committee of the 20th Year of the Republic was appointed by the National Government and has not been abolished to this day. Therefore, the management rights of the Central Stadium are still in the hands of the National Games Preparatory Committee of the 20th Year of the Republic. The preparatory committee consists of more than ten members, all of whom are prominent figures in the Party and state, such as Wei Daoming, Jiang Menglin, and Wang Zhengting. Most of them have left the capital for other destinations. Therefore, the committee has not held any meetings since the September 18th Incident. A small number of staff members are stationed at the attached office in the Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum Administration Office to manage the Central Stadium. This time, the Ministry of Education, based on the resolutions of the National Sports Conference, stipulated that the National Games would be held at the Central Stadium during the Double Tenth Festival next year and that the ministry would separately organize a preparatory committee to manage the preparations. Since this proposal was approved by the Executive Yuan, the National Games Preparatory Committee of the 20th Year of the Republic has expressed dissatisfaction. A key figure of the standing committee of the National Games Preparatory Committee of the 20th Year of the Republic secretly ordered the Central Stadium not to be handed over to the Ministry of Education until a clear order from the National Government was received, and stated that the preparatory work for next year's National Games should still be managed by the committee. Because of this, the Executive Yuan's resolution has not been formally announced by the National Government after half a month, and the Ministry of Education will have no way to start taking over the Central Stadium and preparing for next year's National Games. As for the proposal to use the stadium to prepare for the establishment of the Central Sports Academy, it is feared that it will also be difficult to realize due to the dispute over the management rights of the stadium.

News of the China Youth Basketball League

(Zhenjiang Correspondent) The cycling competition organized by the Jiangsu Provincial Public Stadium is a first for the provincial capital. New Basketball Tactics (36) (Not Permitted) (Reprinted) Claire Burcky Zhang Guodong Qian Yidong Co-Translation

Coach Ralph Wole's Baylor Quintet was the 1932 American Southwest basketball

team. Through experience, they proved that the following tactics are the most effective weapons for attacking zone defenses and man-to-man defenses:

Number 3 slowly dribbles the ball forward, number 4 cuts into the free throw

area, receiving a pass from number 2. At the same time, number 5

immediately cuts across in front of number 4. When the two people (number 4

and number 5) approach, number 4 immediately passes the ball to

number 5 and blocks number 5's defender. At this time, if number 1 has

come out of the surveillance of his defender, then number 5

can pass the ball to number 1, allowing him to shoot

under the basket. Otherwise, he can also shoot on the spot or dribble

in for a shot.

Commercial News

Financial Standard Gold Rises Sharply, Minor Retracement

〓 Falls Back Two Taels and Eight Qian 〓

Yesterday, the upward trend in the market slowed down slightly and then declined again. However, the sharp rise and fall were limited, and the difference between the front and back markets was not significant. The total difference was four taels and three qian. In retrospect, the decline was two taels and eight qian, a reaction to several days of consecutive gains. The market opened with a fall, but the exchange rate rose slightly, and news reported that there might be a proposal to reduce and repay outstanding debts. Therefore, people's minds seemed to be set on further gains. However, there was not much volume in the spot market, and the gold price hovered around 780 taels. Later, the market changed slightly, weakening and then leveling off. Subsequently, the December swap market opened slightly, with Rui Yu and Tong Feng Heng swapping in more than 100 bars, posting a price of two taels and three qian to two taels. Moreover, Duo Fang Ying Feng Heng, Qian Chang Xiang swapped with Da De Cheng and Yuan Mao Yong dozens of bars, posting a price of one tael and a half, which slightly suppressed the red bar, adding only eleven taels and five qian. The current situation is recorded below.

Hovering Around Eighty Taels

From the morning, the January opening price was 780 taels and three qian, immediately dropping one tael and six qian. Subsequently, it added three qian. Because Heng Yu, Heng Chang Yong, and retail investors came to sell, it reached 7,009 taels and six qian. Before long, Fu Yu, Heng Yu, Rui Xing Yuan Yu Yong, Yuan Hou Yong, Yi Feng Yong, and Hui Xiang and others competed to bid, immediately raising the price to eighty-one taels and nine qian. Because Heng Yu, Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Kang Xiang, Zhao Feng Chang, Qian Chang Xiang and others were selling, and because San Bing sold US dollars at 68.75, it retreated more than two taels. At 9:15, it was seventy-nine taels and three qian. Afterwards, Heng Yu, Heng Yu, Rui Xing entered again, and March US dollars closed at 8.75 and made 8.35 again. In January, the exchange rate was 321, instantly reaching eighty taels and nine qian. When HSBC posted the exchange rate, the situation was even more urgent. At this time, Yi Feng Yong and Fu Tai Heng sold, causing the price to fall to seventy-nine taels and four qian. Later, Yuan Mao Yong, Yuan Tai, Zhi Feng Yong, Heng Yu, and Yuan Kang Xiang bought, pulling the price back up more than one tael to eighty-one taels at ten o'clock. After that, it hovered around eighty taels, and the situation was peaceful, but trading was not smooth, and it seemed that there were many suppliers. For US dollars, the price was made at 93.75 on the 3rd, and Heng Yu, Yuan Xing Yong, and Yong Feng waited to be the first to pay. Until 11:15, it was seventy-nine taels and four cents. Then, a group of retail short sellers came to cover, pulling the price back up one tael to eighty taels and a half at 11:30. However, people's minds were unsettled, and the market was not going anywhere. The market closed at noon at seventy-nine taels and six qian.

Weak First, Then Level, Not Much Change

The afternoon market opened at seventy-nine taels and seven qian, followed by eighty taels and one qian, due to Yuan Mao Yong, Rui Xing and others buying in. Suddenly, the central bank sold to Maihang, Huabi, etc. in March US dollars at 125, Huabi gave 93.75 in February and Huiyi gave 75 in January. Bing Xing, Yuan Tai, Zhao Jin Chang, Fu Xing Yong, and Da De Cheng and others sold off, causing a decline of more than two taels. At 2:20, it was seventy-seven taels and six qian. After that, Fu Yu, Zhi Feng Yong, and Rende Cheng came to buy in, and December US dollars closed at 75 again. Then, first let the first half month be convenient, and then the February price recovered, reaching eighty taels and a half at 3:30. Afterwards, the market reversed downstream. Only eight or nine qian rose. Qian Chang Xiang, Zhao Chang, and Dalian helped sell, until it was seventy-eight taels and four qian at 4:00. Finally, US dollars seemed firm, with January made at 8.75, February at 92.75, and Shachi entering again in March. Some retailers were still buying, so the price gradually increased, reaching nine taels and three qian, and then returned to eight taels and seven qian. When the market closed at 4:30, it was nine taels and one qian. Yuan Xing Yong, Yi Feng Yong and others came to buy, so it was hyped up to nine taels and a half. Compared with last Saturday (according to the posted price, the total decline was two taels and eight qian, with the maximum price during the day being eighty-one taels and nine qian and the minimum price being seventy-seven taels and six qian, a difference of four taels and three qian.

Posting Price Lowered by Three Taels

The posting price was still 846 taels, with the amount of press at 66-67 taels to 65-66 taels. In the afternoon, it was 66 taels, then 68 taels, resulting in 67 taels, which was three taels more than last Saturday. Booked twelve months at 86 taels and one month at 80 taels. The month has been cleared, and the supplement water is 82 taels, with 81 taels in the afternoon.

Each Number's Purchases and Sales Are Unpredictable

There were not many spot market transactions in the afternoon. According to statistics, Yuan Mao Yong (Rui Xing agent Qiao Zhifu), Zhi Feng Yong, Yuan Tai, Yuan Kang Xiang, and Fu Yu all entered. Heng Yu had a lot of ups and downs. Heng Chang Yong, Bing Xing, Ying Feng Heng, Yuan Chun, Yong Feng, Zhao Feng Chang, Fu Tai Heng, and Shunli all exited. In the afternoon, Yuan Mao Yong, Heng Yu, Zhi Feng Yong, Rui Xing, Ying Feng Heng, and Yuan Xing Yong all entered. Fu Yu entered 45 hundred bars. The Price of Li Taxes is Balanced, and Transactions are Particularly Smooth

丨Copper Coins Suddenly Contract Again丨

Yesterday, the silver dollar situation showed no significant changes in market prices. However, transactions and settlements were especially smooth and prosperous due to banks reopening on Monday. Given that the Lunar New Year is not far off, most funds cannot advance as boldly as during a period of development. Although things haven’t fully settled, new transactions are naturally not easy to undertake, ultimately leading to a lack of clarity in the situation and a softening of momentum, which is to be expected. Fortunately, overseas sales were quite smooth this time, which is good news amidst the bleakness.

〓Li Prices are Level in the Morning, High at Noon, and the Discount is Relatively Soft〓

The "foreign li" price in the early market was unchanged as buying and selling were vigorous in the morning, with equal strength on both sides. The price remained at 7 mace, 1 fen, 2 li, and 7 hao. In the afternoon market, banks bought more than they sold, and confidence strengthened, resulting in an increase of 2 hao and a half compared to the morning market, to 7 mace, 1 fen, 3 li. The "silver discount" decreased by another 2 fen compared to the previous day, calculated at 4 fen. There was no difference between the morning and afternoon markets. Although the "hua tou" (premium) initially opened at a white price, it closed at 3 or 4 fen.

〓Both Jiao Dollars Rise, Copper Coins Contract Sharply〓

The Jiangnan "small dollar" was 6 mace, 1 fen, and 7 li and a half in the morning market, 1 li and a half higher than the previous afternoon. The afternoon market saw few transactions, with little change. Transactions amounted to 5,500 jiao in the morning and 4,500 jiao in the afternoon. The Guangdong "small dollar" was 6 mace, 1 fen, and 4 li and a half in the morning market, and 6 mace, 1 fen, 5 li, and 7 hao in the afternoon, an increase of 1 li compared to the previous afternoon. Transactions amounted to 135,000 jiao in the morning and 65,000 jiao in the afternoon. Copper coins, which had shown a significant increase the previous day, contracted sharply by 6,000 cash yesterday, a further decrease of 1,000 cash compared to the end of last week, to 397,000 cash. Trading remained strong, with over 40,000 strings of cash.

〓Settlements are Frequent and Transactions are Flourishing〓

Yesterday was Monday, and with the banks reopening, silver dollar transactions and settlements were naturally busy. Chinese merchants' settlement tickets totaled over 3.5 million, foreign merchants' settlement tickets totaled 3.12 million, advances totaled 1 million, special settlements totaled 2.78 million, and active settlements totaled over 5 million. Settlements for various goods, exchange rates, taxes, etc., totaled over 10 million. Issuance totaled 1.5 million, and silver pawn transactions totaled over 1.6 million. Silver public notes from money shops totaled over 37.7 million, "hua song" (transfer) settlements totaled over 5.1 million, various remittances totaled over 900,000, and cash receipts totaled over 1 million. For "foreign accounts," suspended tickets amounted to 1.08 million in the morning and 1.215 million in the afternoon. Banknotes were 85,000 in the morning and 50,000 in the afternoon. Off-market banknotes were 123,000 in the morning and 165,000 in the afternoon. Check transactions were 65,000 in the morning and 35,000 in the afternoon. Bank trading totaled 1.1 million in the morning and 950,000 in the afternoon. Interbank settlements of foreign currency accounts totaled over 1.9 million, banknote withdrawals and issues totaled 1.78 million, foreign currency pawn transactions totaled over 1.1 million, foreign currency public notes from money shops totaled over 10.3 million, "foreign premium" settlements totaled over 2.4 million, and foreign currency borrowing transactions totaled over 2.2 million. Transactions by small money shops totaled over 900,000.

Wenzhou Also Needs Silver Dollars

According to news from the financial community yesterday, Wenzhou's market has always had limited silver dollar reserves. Because the market is small, it does not need a large amount of cash. This time, Liu Zhennian's troops have successively arrived in Wenzhou and are stationed there. The military pay is usually given in Shandong and Luyu bonds. However, the southern market has never used them. The provincial government has ordered the area to use them according to the market.

To build confidence, they have entrusted the financial community to set up collection points.

Therefore, they have telegraphed to the financial community in Shanghai to successively purchase silver dollars and send them to Wenzhou. Yesterday, the first batch of 150,000 was shipped out. Today, they will have to ship another 30,000 to 50,000 in sequence. In addition, yesterday's shipments included 200,000 to Guangzhou, 400,000 to various ports along the Yangtze River, 200,000 to Jinan, 300,000 to Shantou and Xiamen, and 100,000 to the interior. Altogether, including the amount shipped to Wenzhou, the total was 1.35 million. Furthermore, yesterday, various ports collected 200,000 to 300,000, but they were all odd lots, so there are no accurate statistics.

The Price of Securities and Bonds Continues to Rise Sharply

丨The January Futures are Almost Fully Opened丨

丨The Market is Closed Today for Settlement丨

Today, the 29th, the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange will temporarily suspend trading due to the settlement of the November futures contracts. As for yesterday's market conditions, the turnover of spot goods remained sparse, but the January futures contracts for next year, although it was the first day of trading, were almost fully opened, except for Customs 96 and financial stocks. This situation has not been seen in recent years. Market prices have rebounded rapidly, and the enthusiasm of buyers and sellers shows no sign of waning. Not only is the turnover of December futures contracts quite large, but the newly opened January contracts are also very active, not like the usual wait-and-see attitude during settlement periods. The changes in the price of various bonds continue to show a very good situation. Market sentiment is very good, and everyone is inclined to buy, which has led to unusually enthusiastic buying. As a result, various prices have continued to rise sharply. In the two morning sessions, there were no major changes compared to the end of last week, but in the afternoon market, prices rose sharply, more than one yuan higher than the morning. As a result, 20 Customs bonds rose by 1.5 yuan, and consolidated salt tax 20 bonds rose by over 1 yuan each, while the whole 6 bonds rose sharply by 2.2 yuan, and others also rose by 6 or 7 jiao each. Total spot trading for the day amounted to 28,000 yuan, and futures trading amounted to 7.7 million yuan, of which new January trading accounted for over 1.1 million yuan.

New York Stock Market Mixed

Xinfeng Foreign Firm reports that on Saturday (the 26th) the New York stock market first rose due to progress in railway freight. Then, speculators took advantage of the high prices to sell, so the price recovered to fatigue, and the result was no significant change from the previous day. Half-day turnover totaled 376,000 shares. Also, Railway Magazine reported that freight cars increased by 77,652 within a week, a new record for the year. The stock market this week was almost entirely dominated by the war debt issue. Although the selling pressure was evident on Wednesday, turnover was not large. Because the shares are partly in the hands of the public, otherwise the market would have collapsed long ago. It is expected that war debt will remain the central force before December 15. However, Congress will convene soon. If the budget bill has good results, the bad international situation can be offset. Otherwise, the market trend may break through the low of October 11. The closing prices of the Dow Jones Indexes on the 26th are listed below:

Cotton Yarn Market Enters a Slump

The cotton yarn market is trending downwards, and the situation is extremely bleak. Actual sales are too sluggish, and the financial depletion in the interior is unimaginable. In addition, inferior yarns are being dumped at reduced prices in all directions, further affecting local yarns. As a result, business has been cut off, and the backlog of each factory is increasing day by day. The future situation is grim. The Shenxin Factory sees the unfavorable environment and opens sales from time to time. Buyers are hedging their bets in the futures market.

The Human Mark Market is Pessimistic

The opening of the human mark market was declining due to American trends. Sentiment remained at a decline of 3 to 4 mace for each month. It was reported that there were still few transactions in the afternoon, and each month fell by another 1, 2, and 5 mace. Total market turnover was estimated at 15,000 bales. It was found that Dafu sold 600 bales, Jifeng sold 850 bales, Jianyu sold 700 bales, Yicheng sold 700 bales, and Yichang sold 450 bales. Cotton Market is Gradually Softening

The cotton market is gradually showing signs of weakening. Because American cotton is completely lifeless, and yarn and cloth are falling, spot sales are stagnant. The price of cotton in Hankou is said to be falling. Thus, the situation is turning tired, and the decline is slightly intense. However, the supply from various sources is still lacking. The future situation is difficult to grasp.

Grain and Rice Market is Slightly Stable

(South) Yesterday, more than fifty merchants came from various regions. Trading in the area was more active than usual. Northern accounts were slightly above stack, close to a thousand piculs. Prices rose slightly. Early and late, sales followed arrivals, and the situation stabilized. Arriving goods were weak, and prices were tired.

(News) Approximately thirty-seven or eight rice boats arrived. Local defense sales were brisk. Rice fell 2 jiao. Rice merchants from Changshu and Jiangyin were slightly active, and prices stabilized. Goods at the pier were neither glorious nor disgraced.

Customer Xiang Rice Sales Strong and Prices Rise

丨Geng Yang Gang is Extremely Poor丨

Yesterday, the customer Xiang rice market was stagnant in the north and booming in the south. Arrivals continued to come at a price, which was due to the Nangyang gang's extremely keen taste for millet. The Erzhou and Quanzhou areas were the first to inquire. Recently, because foreign rice is not economical, the intention to deal is stronger. Yesterday, in addition to Quanzhou and Fuzhou, the Shantou and Xiamen gangs followed up and competed for sales, and prices jumped up by five or six cents, close to the jiao. Based on the strong appetite of the Nantou gang, the market should rise in steps. However, because there are large amounts of foreign rice in storage in the market and many new arrivals of customer Xiang rice, Hunan rice can be continuously shipped to Shanghai after the production price is aligned. Jiangxi rice is also aligned recently, so there is no need to worry about shortages. Because the source is not interrupted, the market price will not see a sharp increase. Sales follow arrivals, and there is no large-scale accumulation in the market. Yesterday, Tongshi opened sales of 1,000 bags of Hunan machine oil at prices of 8 yuan 8 jiao 7 fen and 8 yuan 7 jiao 24 fen, down to 8 yuan 6 jiao. Also, 650 bags of machine red rice were priced at 8 yuan 5 fen to 7 yuan 9 jiao. Also, 100 bags of red crude were priced at 6 yuan 9 jiao 7 fen. Also, 550 bags of Jingshan were priced at 7 yuan 2 jiao 7 fen to 7 yuan 2 jiao. 800 bags of Jiangxi machine late were priced at 8 yuan 9 jiao to 8 yuan 6 jiao.

Future Wheat is Cleverly Housed

丨Only Seven Cars of Wheat Delivered This Month丨

Yesterday, the future wheat market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, generally showed a firm trend for each month. Foreign wheat was good, and the sale of spot foreign wheat has also recently been quiet. (However, there are rumors that Australian wheat is sold out of warehouses for 3 taels, 3 qian, and 8 fen, but the authenticity is unknown.) In addition, futures trading has been firmly suppressed by large factories, and the steps are rising. The source of wheat has also been limited recently, so sentiment has been brought up. As a result, January was 4 fen better than the previous day, February had no comparison, March was 4 fen better, and April was 3 fen. The number of deliveries this month was limited, totaling only 7 cars, delivered by Yuanyu Dingmai, etc., and received by Yuanhechang, said to have been handled by Huafeng.

Near Firm and Far Even Flour Market

Yesterday's flour market, after opening in the morning and afternoon, showed a trend of near firm and far even for each month. The price of foreign wheat rebounded by one jiao, and manufacturers, especially small and medium-sized factories, had a prospect. Those who have entered the factory are now reluctant to sell because the spot goods are still tight, so the situation this month is still firm and clever. Luo Gao is at 1 tael, 8 qian, and 6 fen. December and January also showed gains. Early in the long-term months, it was also firm, but by the afternoon, sentiment softened again due to some selling by Fu. Looking at the recent trend, because the gold market is more expensive and the exchange rate is shortening, the general public believes that foreign wheat orders will be hit. However, if foreign products are still surplus, I am afraid no one will care. As a result, the months from this month to January rose by 1 fen, February and March rose by 2 li, and April rose by 5 li.

Silk and Tea District Continues to Ship to Shanghai

丨240 Pieces Arrived by Small Steamer Yesterday丨

The sales route of the Ji Li District to Europe and America has been difficult to smooth for a long time, and since the new silk has been listed in the producing area, each silk firm has handed over the new silk to the factory, the old swing became jing, the silk in storage has increased sharply, and the canal is quite lively. Yesterday (Nanxun) (Huhu) two ports, there were 240 pieces of Qianjing, which were transported to Shanghai by small steamer and stored in stacks for sale.

Foreign Tea Market Turns Quiet

Yesterday, the foreign tea market in this port turned quiet. The most important Luju Zhenmei sales route was quite sluggish. Tu tea and Pearl tea had scattered transactions. The market has been in a depressed mood. The Contribution Tea was reopened by the Russian Assistance Association's foreign firm yesterday. However, the amount of entering the stomach is not very recognized, and the price is still low. General tea merchants are still pessimistic about the future of the tea market.

21 Branch Talk

Textual Research on Wu Proverbs

— Zhanlu

The grammar of Wu proverbs has no specialized book, only in tacit understanding. In describing time, Wu proverbs sometimes use "tou li" (頭裏) and sometimes "tou shang" (頭上). 丨Shang is pronounced as Lang, same below.

Suddenly is called "zha sheng tou li" (乍生頭裏), in a dream is called "kun meng tou li" (困夢頭裏), in disappointment is called "dao mei tou li" (倒霉頭裏), in busyness is called "jia mang tou li" (夾忙頭裏); all sudden or unfortunate events are applicable to these two words "tou li."

In important times it is called "yao jin tou shang" (要緊頭上), when fortune arrives it is called "yun qi tou shang" (運氣頭上), when delicious it is called "hao chi tou shang" (好吃頭上), at a crucial moment it is called "guan zi tou shang" (關子頭上); all important or fortunate events are applicable to these two words "tou shang."

The people of Suzhou are glib, and many of the transmitted proverbs have been misinterpreted; I have corrected their errors from the aspect of "a change of one sound," and I very much want to write a correction of Wu proverbs to correct the dialects of my hometown. Now I will write a few items behind:

It is commonly said that there is no hope, called "yao chang meng dong" (杳長懞懂); it should be corrected to "ye chang meng duo" (夜長夢多, long night, many dreams). It is commonly said that things are entangled, called "ya ge luan jing" (丫割亂經), it should be corrected to "wo ge nong jing" (握葛弄荆, holding kudzu and playing with thorns). It is commonly said that misunderstandings occur, called "chuan zui jia zhong" (傳嘴夾中), it should be corrected to "chan zhi jiao niu" (纏枝絞紐, entangled branches and twisted knots). It is commonly said to wear clothes loosely, called "san pao san jia" (散抛散夾), it should be corrected to "san pao san jia" (散袍散甲, scattered robes and armor). It is commonly said to waste things, called "ang zang ma yi" (骯髒螞蟻, dirty ants); 丨Yi is pronounced as Mi. It should be corrected to "ang zang mo mie" (骯髒磨滅, dirty attrition).

In slang, people like to use the three characters "ba zhi jiao" (八隻脚, eight feet). Too far away is called "dang kong ba zhi jiao" (蕩空八隻脚, empty space eight feet), too many people and hands are called "qi shou ba zhi jiao" (七手八隻脚, seven hands eight feet), too many branches are called "ya cha ba zhi jiao" (丫叉八隻脚, forked eight feet); 丨Yi is pronounced as Qiang. Disorderly is called "shi chai ba zhi jiao" (拾柴八隻脚, pick firewood eight feet); 丨Shi is pronounced as Xi.

The origin of "shi chai ba zhi jiao" (拾柴八隻脚) comes from the four characters "shi chai po zhou" (拾柴潑粥, pick firewood and spill porridge), which have been misinterpreted through transmission; just because the speech is glib, "shi chai po zhou" (拾柴潑粥) is read as "shi chai ba zu" (拾柴八足, pick firewood eight feet), and the pronunciation of the characters has already been misinterpreted; unexpectedly, one mistake leads to another, and the two characters "ba zu" (八足, eight feet) are misinterpreted as "ba zhi jiao" (八隻脚, eight feet). Therefore, in Wu proverbs, there is this five-character noun "shi chai ba zhi jiao" (拾柴八隻脚).

Contradictory Facts

— Zhu Lu

Under the sign of "Winter Sale," old, young, male, and female, like a tide, crowded the various departments of the Three Companies and the big department stores; silver and banknotes flowed continuously into the copper counters, and big and small packages were continuously tucked under the armpits of those old and young, male and female customers. Crowded together, where can one still find the phenomenon of "business slump" in the Shanghai market after three or four in the afternoon?

On the road where the red and green iridescent lights shone, the beauty cars adorned with carbide lamps, the cool night was like water, and the wind penetrated the skin at midnight, shuttled back and forth on the road. The small electric lights, like the twinkling stars in the sky, were just as lively and prosperous. This scene of prosperity is truly gilded and intoxicating. Who can still say that China is not peaceful!

"The heart of patriotism, dare not lag behind others." "Economic severance, persevere to the end." Shanghai, which is full of patriotic merchants, has recently had 300,000 inferior goods selling well in the Shanghai market. "The world is bustling, all for profit; the world is bustling, all for profit." No wonder the bombs of the blood soul group cannot revive the conscience of that group of patriotic merchants! The afterglow of the "Kalachakra Mandala Ceremony" has just subsided, and the XX Department is promoting the national quintessence of dragon boat racing again. No wonder the "high pavilion" of Sanbei has received a notice from the provincial government for protection; the "Yansheng Association" in Wuxi has caused a sensation among tens of thousands of people. This is one time, that is another time. The gears of the times are constantly cycling forward. Who knows that during this period of national crisis, the old immortals on the top of Kunyu Mountain will not descend gracefully and ask the heavenly soldiers and generals to kill all the foreign invaders for the Republic of China.

There are too many contradictory things, which is how the Republic of China is organized into a national crisis, but the Heng dance and the drunken song remain.

Central Idea of Movies and Dramas

— Xiuqing

丨Need Revolutionary Stimulation丨

The narration of love stories. In the current diverse movies and dramas, it has almost become the only central drama material. No matter whether it is a domestic or foreign film, sound or silent, almost seven or eight out of ten jump out of this circle. Mei Lanfang arrived in Shanghai today. Mr. Mei has been invited by all circles to come south, but he declined and failed to get it. He may perform voluntarily for a few days. According to a special telegram from Beiping, Mr. Mei has already gone south by Yongche and is scheduled to arrive at the North Station at 5:30 p.m. , and everything has been taken care of by Mr. Huang Jinrong, and we will go to meet him.

For example, "Human Beast Wonders" is just a news-oriented beast film. But the insertion of the explorer's love story is still an indispensable material.

Originally, drama is the performance of life. Love is also the most interesting and meaningful section in the life process. Of course, this is the only good drama material for making movies. However, in every film. There is no correct and noble central idea, specializing in catering to the audience's low-level psychology by favoring romantic, amorous and sensual performances. This is a very common disease in current Chinese and Western films. At the same time, it can also be said to be a sign of the decline of the film industry.

Especially during the national crisis, under the creed of "entertainment does not forget to save the country." What the public urgently needs is definitely not the anesthetizing films of individual hedonism; but a type of work with a revolutionary patriotic thought.

However, domestic films of this type are really rare and very few in number. Here, we cannot but praise the recent sound film "Flower of Freedom" written and directed by Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu of the Star Film Company. The plot of this film is about General Cai Songpo overthrowing the monarchy and recreating the revolutionary story of the Republic. Endless patriotic blood and tears are reflected on the screen. The great spirit of fighting for freedom is depicted in the film, which is very stimulating. The profound performance of the protagonist, Ms. Hu Die, makes the emotions feel more real and moving. Indeed, this is a film and drama that is needed by the times and is different from the current trend.

Occasional Notes on Reading Paintings

— Deng Qingcheng

In the spring of the year before last in my county, I initiated the Yunxi Painting and Calligraphy Association, which brought together more than 500 pieces of works by painters and calligraphers in the county. It was exhibited in the first public garden for ten days, and it was very grand at the time. Afterwards, there was no shortage of people who continued, but there were many landscapes, figures, and freehand flowers and birds, each with its own characteristics and different schools of painting. However, if you want to be like Mr. Zhao Anzhi who has devoted himself to it for more than 20 years, from the Song and Yuan Dynasties to the Ming and Qing Dynasties, he has copied all the masters to the fullest extent and achieved the ultimate, which is very worthwhile to watch. Mr. Zhao, although a native of the county, has been away for a long time. He is proficient in landscapes, figures, and feather and animal painting. In the past, he participated in the National Art Exhibition and the Belgian Ryan Chess International Exposition, and both won high praise and won gold awards, so he has long been famous at home and abroad. This month, when he returned to his hometown, he first displayed his large and small masterpieces in the park. I was able to participate in the grand event, and I deeply admire his hard work, which is difficult and valuable. There are many inscriptions by famous people, such as Mr. Kuang Zhoufeng's inscription on the Painting of Heavenly Maid Scattering Flowers, adjusted to the tune of Qing Buluo: In the country of many fragrances, is the heavenly maid or not? But it was Qingniao who made the messenger, saying that it was Fairy E'e. I pity Duo Bing Xiuwen, Vimalakirti's previous life, drawing the truth and calling him to wake up, and he will start to make spring. Mr. Chu Minyi inscribed a flower and bird album saying: Lifelike. Mr. Wang Yiting inscribed: The fragrance of flowers and the language of birds adorn the spring breeze, and the wonderful brush imitates nature, the light green and deep red are beautiful in spring, and it is beyond the image to get in the middle. Mr. Zhu Xibai inscribed plum blossoms: The spring letter from Gushan arrives at the southern branches, and the snow is more gorgeous than peach and plum blossoms. Mr. He Jing should smile, and his old wife still likes to fight Yan Zhi. I also inscribed a quatrain on the lotus I wrote: A famous flower that can overwhelm the country cannot withstand autumn, this flower is like a brocade, and its nature is secluded. Don't dislike that there are no good works in the late evening, but it occupies the first place in the cold river. Others such as Qian Mingshan's inscription on the postscript of peach blossom hydrangea, and Wu Jingyu's inscription on daffodils and bluebirds, are all extremely clear and exquisite. Even Anzhi's own inscription on the painting is also full of beautiful sentences. On the third day of the exhibition, the viewers gathered, all thinking that the painting style has been greatly revived. Compared with those who make current paintings with a free brush, it cannot be compared.

The Crossroads of Death

— Fan Yanqiao (2)(10)(8)

Such an Ending

From room number 436 of the Southeast Hotel, a perfect couple walked out, the woman like a blossoming flower, clinging to the man's arm. The man constantly twitched his little mustache, laughing with unrestrained pride. At the elevator entrance, they switched directions, standing opposite each other. The man was about to brush aside a strand of hair on the woman's forehead, but she turned her head and twisted the ends of her hair into a small circle herself, then turned back to ask, "How is it?" The man nodded and said, "Good!" The woman said again, "These few strands of hair never seem to hold a curl, almost curling them every day, but they still hang straight down."

The elevator arrived, taking them both to the sixth floor. The rooms on the sixth floor were larger and more elaborately furnished. Room number 666 was the most opulent, and they walked into this one. The bellboy recognized Aili and smiled knowingly, not asking any questions. Whether it was tea or cigarettes, he knew to bring them. As soon as he slammed the door shut, the man eagerly asked, "Aili, have you promised me?" Aili, still facing the mirror, fiddled with the hair circles on her forehead and said softly, "Why so impatient? Marriage is a lifelong commitment, one must consider it carefully, right?" "Muliang! I want to ask you, you like women so much, is there only a female dog guarding your house? I don't believe it!" "I can swear on that, if I have a concubine at home, I'll..." Aili hurriedly rushed over, covering his mouth with her hand, saying, "Don't say it! I believe you." She seized the opportunity to sit on his lap, lowering her head to look at the whorls on her fingers. Muliang brought his little mustache closer, closer to her cheek, and stopped. Aili pushed him away, stood up, and sat down in the rocking chair opposite, saying with a tremble in her voice, "Suppose, a country girl, a big, snowy bun of hair, two large sleeves swaying back and forth, would you be willing to kiss her?"

Muliang chuckled and said, "How could you imagine such a thing? Seeing her would make me want to throw up my dinner from the night before, how could I have the appetite to kiss her?"

"So you like modern tricks, can even speak foreign languages, then you'll despise me, won't you?" Muliang quickly defended, "No! Never! In short, you have already satisfied my desires." "Suppose, the current me, returns to my original appearance, you wouldn't want me then, would you?"

"What is your original appearance like?"

"A country girl!"

"Hmm!... In short, right now I only love you, you can change, change, change, even into a yaksha, and I would still love you."

"Really?"

"Really!"

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Selling Old Age

— Tian Fang

In recent days, the newspapers have been carrying huge advertisements, claiming that a "long-bearded Daoist of one hundred and nine years who once ate a giant peach" is "cultivating longevity connections" within X World, "available for anyone to see, no admission fee." Those who cherish the three blessings [longevity, wealth, and health] will surely flock to him, seeking instructions from this "quasi-immortal" on the secrets of longevity, or perhaps even taking him as a master, in order to ascend to the realm of immortality together. This is a once-in-a-millennium opportunity.

Originally, this world is pitifully small and strangely incomplete. A lifespan of just a few decades cannot satisfy human desires. But to seek longevity, one must enter the mountains and "cultivate the Dao for sixty years," which is an unaccustomed loneliness. The mountains are not like the mountains of Tangshan or Moganshan, where one can ride in a car and eat good food. This is what modern people are unwilling to do. Seeking longevity for the sake of "enjoying pleasure," yet wanting to "suffer" first in order to achieve longevity, this business seems too uneconomical. Therefore, the comedy of entering the mountains to cultivate the Dao is only undertaken by a few "without a path to life" or fools. Dignified gentlemen would never fall for that. Now it's good, the immortal doesn't abandon the mortal world, descends to the foreign concessions, and for a small fee of two cents, one can obtain the secret of longevity, truly the cheapest and most beautiful thing. Moreover, it's much more useful than life insurance that makes the descendants rich after death. Presumably, "white teeth" can be "reborn," and youthful beauty will naturally not be difficult to maintain. From then on, people will be "floating," and everyone will have "three-foot-long beards," with old men all over the streets. This would become like the "Nation of Wisdom" in "Flowers in the Mirror," what a grand event! By that time, "eightieth birthday celebrations" would become a joke, and even "thousand-elder banquets" would be insignificant.

But I also think that the meaning of life does not lie in the length of life, but in how much responsibility one bears for the advancement of the times and society. If one only seeks to be "old and not die," that's a "quirk," and there's really not much meaning to it. Therefore, Wang Yi died for his country, and though his life was short, it was like heaven's lifespan, while Peng Zu lived to eight hundred, and though his life was long, it was like a day. Boasting about lifespan to the earth is really pitifully short. The cicada does not know spring and autumn, yet the great transformation of the universe remains a mystery to mankind to this day. Therefore, there is no need to ask for directions, just walk step by step. To put it another way, even if a person lives to be a hundred or a thousand years old, besides being charmingly senile and available for people to admire, what else is the use? What is the difference between this and the "ancient treasures" in the Palace Museum? In terms of intrinsic value, they are probably not as worthy as Zhou tripods and Yin basins that can be sold.

China is essentially a youthful country. Most of the administrators are young, handsome, learned, and capable, rarely are they elderly and senile. Although some have long beards, they have never reached three feet, and the general mentality is that when one is not yet seventy, one should retire to the forests and springs, spending one's remaining years in leisure. Taking on great difficulties is a matter for the younger generation. Like the German President Paul von Hindenburg, who at the age of eighty-five still held the power of the entire country, handling ten thousand things a day, not knowing to retire and enjoy a few years of peace in his hometown, he is truly the world's biggest fool.

Alas, Eastern and Western cultures are ultimately separated by an ocean.
