Scientific Knowledge

A New Method for Measuring Tone Fork Vibration Frequencies

— Rui Yucheng

Acoustics scholars all know what a tuning fork is, and they all know its importance. The point of its importance is because its tone resembles the club that produces the original sound; the harmonic overtones it produces are few. Therefore, those measuring the vibration frequencies of various musical instruments often use tuning forks as the standard. Thus, the need for accuracy in tuning fork vibration frequency is beyond saying. But common methods for measuring tuning fork vibration frequency are nothing more than the following:

(1) Selecting various tuning forks of known vibration frequency and vibrating them simultaneously with a certain fork; when it is measured that the pitches of the sounds are the same, the known vibration frequency is the vibration frequency of that certain tuning fork. (2) Using a siren and vibrating it alongside a fork, adjusting its speed so that it is consistent with the pitch of the fork; the vibration frequency of the certain fork is inferred from the rotational speed and the number of holes on the plate.

(3) Coating a cylinder or glass plate with lampblack or white powder, attaching a very thin needle to the end of the fork, making the needle tip lightly contact the cylinder or plate, and after striking the fork to vibrate it, rotating the cylinder or moving the plate at a uniform speed, the number of waves drawn by the fork can be measured within a certain time, and its vibration frequency can also be inferred.

Although the above three methods use both ears and eyes, they tend to rely more on the ears. The newest measuring method, however, emphasizes the use of eyes and uses ears as an aid, and its theory is more meticulous; therefore, I specifically

Page 18

Shen Bao Local Supplement

wrote it out, to enrich reference materials for colleagues.

(1) Take the tuning fork whose vibration frequency is to be measured and vibrate it at the same time as a string; and look at the vibration state of the string through the gaps between the prongs of the fork. If the two vibration frequencies are indeed equal, then the back-and-forth vibration of the string will present a kind of roundabout and slow phenomenon, which can be seen from the side. If the two are slightly mismatched, there will be no such situation at all. Readjust the length and tension of the string, so that this phenomenon is very obvious, and then use the string vibration frequency formula to calculate the vibration frequency of the string, which is the vibration frequency of the tuning fork.

(2) Connect the siren plate to a rotator and rotate it at a uniform speed, and place the tuning fork in front of the plate, allowing a portion of the plate to be seen through the gaps between the fork prongs; if the vibration frequencies of the sounds emitted by the two are indeed equal, then the round holes on the plate will appear to be stationary and not rotating; if there is a slight difference, then the round holes will seem to slowly move either backwards or forwards, and the speed of their movement will differ depending on the difference between the two vibration frequencies. Therefore, know that if you adjust the siren to produce the above phenomenon, and then use the siren calculation method to find its vibration frequency, you will get the vibration frequency of the tuning fork.

(3) Take the tuning fork whose vibration frequency is to be measured and a tuning fork of known vibration frequency, making their prongs directly parallel to each other...place a candle flame behind the second tuning fork. Strike the two forks to make them sound, and observe the flame with one eye from the gap between the two forks...If the two vibration frequencies are indeed equal, then the flame will appear and disappear at certain intervals and in a regular rhythm; if there is a slight difference, then the appearance and disappearance of the light will not be in sync; it may even be confused and invisible. Therefore, test with various forks until a regular phenomenon occurs. Then the vibration frequency of the known fork is the vibration frequency of the unknown fork.

The above three new methods can correct the errors of hearing with eyesight; because hearing often fails to discern subtle differences, scholars must use multiple methods for testing, referencing and comparing, in order to obtain accurate results!

Class Amusement Meeting

— Lianlian

Excitedly walking into the classroom, a blackboard eraser suddenly fell and hit my head with a "thump," making sparks fly from the top of my head. Just as I was about to explode, the students inside shouted, "Today's amusement meeting has no admission fee, and a blackboard eraser is included!" So I calmed down, knowing that this class was ruled by the barber's assistant, and there would definitely be some very fresh tricks to be discovered. Sure enough, after settling down and looking up, the blackboard was already filled with the program, which included:

Little Long-legs Violin Solo

Tailor's Assistant Gongche Tune

Bull Tricks and Horse Show

Ms. XXX Sings Lullaby

Young Mistress Hypnotic Song

Three "Tang" Joint Trial

Mr. XXX Humming Tune

Mass March

................................................................

Good, with so many good programs and good music to listen to for an hour, probably no one will doze off. So after the teacher took attendance, Little Long-legs' ghostly and lingering mouth-skill violin, followed by the tailor's assistant's strange Gongche tune, took the stage. With the accompaniment of music, the teacher spoke with even more color. The students in the hall were filled with a spring breeze, and the barber's assistant worked without hearing it.

When the yellow bull and the old horse began to move, they knocked over a desk. Because of their failure, they declared, "We are unable to offer our poor performance today, please teach us tomorrow, please forgive us." After saying that, the masculine lady XXX blew her reed and performed a lullaby. Little Tang, with two eyes staring, couldn't help but conduct some "oiling." "Ai!" Little Tang had to withdraw his hand, smiling at everyone around him.

Originally, the next program was the young mistress's hypnotic song. However, the young mistress avoided the scene at the last minute. The young mistress's black lacquer stool, Gu Lao, (Gu should be written as orphan) then said to the crowd, "She is indisposed today, please forgive her..."

Unfortunately, Little Tang in the Three "Tang" Joint Trial, because he had just wanted to oil but was shouted back by everyone, deliberately took the stage to make trouble, causing the small head with a Pingju addiction in the training ground to be quite disappointed.

Mr. XXX was very generous, and the humming tune was finally hummed out. This so-called Mr. is not a real Mr., but because he has the style of a Mr., he is called that. He sang the humming tune very well, and congratulatory telegrams flew in like snowflakes. He untied his cravat triumphantly.

The teacher held fast to the principle of "sing if you want, but I still teach," only speaking eloquently, and pretending not to hear even if he did.

March of the Grandees, boom boom... boom boom boom```, the entire classroom singing loudly startled the teacher. So he gave a lecture to the students in Mandarin, but the program had already been performed in order, and the merits were also said to be complete. The students laughed out loud and squeezed out like a tide with the dismissal bell.

A Letter

— Cai Xuan

My Ling:

Like a wisp of spider silk in mid-air, you have once again drifted alone to distant Guangzhou. As your wife, your Chan should have given you deep comfort and sympathy for your wandering, but your Chan has not done so, and not only has she not felt lonely because of your departure, but she has also learned to be much quieter!

My Ling! There is no need for you to resent or grieve after reading these few sentences, because undeniably, we are no longer as passionately in love as we were during our courtship; we are growing more and more distant and estranged!

Since we had our lovely and pitiful Ying'er, for various reasons, it marked the beginning of our estrangement and alienation. This estrangement and alienation gradually grew, and your Chan gradually lost her usual love for you, and even became a little disgusted with you! Because of this, I often remain silent, treasure my smile, sadly show my unhappy face, don't talk to you happily, and often curse you for a little trivial matter for no reason, and finally sob and cry to you! As for you? Ah, pitiful Ling, you seem to be deeply depressed after seeing my abnormal attitude towards you, but you did not comfort and inquire me with tenderness as you did in the past when I was angry, you just remained silent, which proves that you are also harboring a hatred of me! Especially when we sleep silently in bed, I always sternly refuse your physiological demands on me, which further increases your anger, and you often vent the anger that cannot be vented on our beloved Ying'er, who is pitiful, lonely, and cold. Thus, in such a situation, there is no joy, no laughter, everything presents the gloomy atmosphere of autumn, and the family that we once recognized as happy has become a painful family!

Dear Ling, I feel very painful and very sad that our relationship has broken down! Therefore, I often shed my tears and sadly recall the sweetness and perfection of our past life, and now, alas, it is truly unbearable to look back, unbearable to look back!

I still remember deeply when I was in the maiden days of my flowery youth, a kind of natural, hot, youthful vitality made me unable to control myself and I longed for a handsome lover. Later, I finally met you, I felt happy, and at that time I truly loved you deeply! Soon, after much difficulty, we were able to struggle out from under the iron heel of our old family and get married. However, after living such a happy life for less than a year, we both felt somewhat ordinary; however, at that time we still hoped that a lovely child would regulate our ordinary and lonely life; but I was disappointed, after I gave birth to Ying'er, the child's crying, the complexity of household affairs,...all of this made me gradually feel disgusted from ordinary! At the same time, I gradually felt that you were not as lovely as before! Everything about you would arouse my dissatisfaction and disgust. Therefore, we became estranged, alienated, creating this irreparable and unfortunate situation.

Now what? For the sake of life, you have once again drifted alone to distant Guangzhou. Although I have not given you comfort and sympathy, in my heart I still love you on the emotional basis of our several years of marriage! We are still young, and there are many more years of cohabitation to come. I hope that we can all try our best to rekindle the dead ashes of love, and not continue this ominous situation. Yes, my Ling, I love you, I still deeply love you; you also understand me, you also deeply love me, right!

Ying'er has become more interesting, clever, and lively recently, please don't worry! Your Chan.

Essays

— Wu Wei

If your secret is known by more than two people, then your secret will definitely not be able to be kept, because people's mouths cannot be tied shut!

Don't think that a disabled or physically incomplete person is completely useless, because a disabled person is always more useful than a corpse buried in the dirt!

If you want to praise a person or a thing, it is best to do so after everything is over, so-called "the coffin is closed, the judgment is made," because everything is constantly changing until the very end, and no one can predict in advance.

The happiness of life is not money, but a healthy body and a life without losing virtue.

The true face of a so-called modern woman: is only completely revealed in the fleeting moment when she gets out of bed in the morning, because usually she is always under a cover of makeup.

She in Sickness

— Luan Xue

This is a rainy night in early winter. The cold wind howls outside the house, and the rain patters against the glass windows. The room is as silent as death. All the people are chasing their good dreams, only the sick her is awake at this time. Her pale face, rapid breathing, and sunken, lifeless eyes show that she is terminally ill.

She often falls asleep in a daze and loses consciousness, knowing that she is not far from death, but she is not terrified or sad, because the stimuli she has received are too deep. She hopes for the early arrival of death, so that she can escape from pain and bid farewell to this man-eating society forever. Her eyes are looking at the top of the tent, longing for all her past! A dreamlike life, in her weak mind, suddenly arises boundless feelings.

How beautiful her childhood was. Her kind grandmother, dear father and mother, how much they cherished her. At that time, she was like a happy angel, living happy days without worry or sorrow. But how long ago was that? Her grandmother died, and her father also fell ill and never recovered. Evil fate began from then on. For their own selfishness, her older brother and sister-in-law urged her mother to marry her off. Her mother also hoped that she would find a place to settle down soon, in order to fulfill her long-cherished wish. As the saying goes, "When the father dies, the older brother is in charge." She could not help but be independent. From then on, she lost her freedom and sacrificed her life's happiness.

The wickedness of her mother-in-law, the unscrupulousness of her husband, and the life of a slave for several years made her suffer countless torments and pains. Several times she wanted to commit suicide, but when she thought of her elderly mother, she was afraid that she would suffer in pregnancy, so she did not have the courage to commit suicide. Not long ago, she gave birth to a boy, but unfortunately, because of congenital deficiency, he went to heaven in a few days, and her treatment after that was even more unimaginable; her heart, which had been deeply hurt, could no longer withstand the postpartum torment.

She thought of the happiness of her childhood, the loveliness of her girlhood, but now everything is over. Her youth has long since passed, and her active mind has long since died. Even this last breath is still lingering in pain. Ah! Who made her like this? Whose fault? Whose fault...

The rain was weeping pattering, and the wind was howling as if it was unfair to her. Her consciousness gradually blurred in the sound of the wind howling and the rain.

Film Special Edition

Actor's Self-Narration

What Does It Mean to Be an "Actor"?

— Ai

How convenient it is to be an actor, as long as you can laugh and cry, right? No, no, it's definitely more than that.

Actors can be divided into two types, one is the puppet-style actor, and the other is the actor with a soul. What is a puppet-style actor? An actor is completely alienated from the script he or she is performing, and even does not understand at all what class, what environment, and what personality the character he or she is playing is. He or she is just listening to the director's instructions and temporarily becomes a genius puppet. An actor with a soul not only has a considerable understanding of the character in the play he or she is portraying, but also clearly understands the entire script and the personalities of all the characters in the play: a director's affairs are naturally more complex than an actor's by more than ten times, so sometimes there are inevitably places that cannot be taken care of. This is the responsibility of every actor. Such an actor must have a soul, and only with a soul can he or she become an actor.

Although I know that an actor has a soul, I strive to understand society and everything in the play, but this is really a difficult task, and I cannot bear my responsibility! The responsibility of an actor.

I once wrote a script, and I hope that in my own script I can gradually become an actor. It is extremely ridiculous to say that the script I wrote is nothing more than a portrait of myself. I really don't know how many facts I will have to write about in the future; now I am starting to write the second script, and there are two other scripts still in the planning stage.

Reader's Opinions

Regarding Subtitles in Sound Films

— Yi Lie

Pay Attention to Actions, Reduce Subtitles

Modern Chinese sound films cannot achieve excellent results, and we should forgive them, because sound films in China are still in their infancy! Therefore, filming techniques and various experiences are naturally not comparable to those of the elder brother, Hollywood.

Let me talk about the subtitles in modern Chinese sound films.

First, let's talk about foreign sound films. Apart from the names of the production company, director, and actors at the beginning of the film, subtitles are rarely seen. Only in extremely tortuous plots are a few subtitles written to explain!

Speaking of our Chinese sound films, in addition to the indispensable subtitles with the company and actor names at the beginning, subtitles are often added in the middle of the main drama to explain actions and facts that are not shown. This is truly superfluous. The audience not only does not find it interesting but also finds it annoying, with no lingering aftertaste. Take the recent Tianyi masterpiece "Traces of the Orchid Valley" as an example. There are many superfluous parts in it, such as "That Night," "Jin Huilan's Family," "Ying Qigui's Family," etc., which are subtitles that viewers find annoying.

The director adds many subtitles intending to explain the plot to viewers who do not understand it; this is the director guessing wrong. The audience's level of understanding of the film may not be as superficial as the director thinks! Moreover, it can also be expressed through dialogue or more filming.

Charlie Chaplin's films are all silent films, but his subtitles are very few, avoiding many unnecessary subtitles as much as possible. However, everyone who has seen his films understands them, which is of course because his actions can replace explanations and express the plot.

Sound films use actions and words to express the plot, and subtitles can be omitted.

Therefore, sound films should avoid many superfluous subtitles. Even in silent films, reducing subtitles and paying attention to the expression of actions instead of subtitles will make the film more interesting and have a lingering aftertaste. I ask the Chinese directors, do you agree?

Search If You Want To

— Ou

Joan Blondell has a strange habit: she likes to search other people's suitcases or handbags. Once, she saw an unfamiliar gentleman holding a small suitcase. She ran over and said to him very enthusiastically, "I beg you to let me search your suitcase. I am willing to pay five dollars for it." She is not a government detective, nor is she trying to discover any secrets or steal anything from people. According to her own words, she simply has this kind of need in her heart.

Casual Chat

The Lack of Comedies in Domestic Films (1)

— Dao Sheng

The lack of comedies in domestic films is reminiscent of the Soviet Union's "Total Mobilization of Laughter."

Comedies make people feel happy, forget their worries, and turn sorrow into joy. Laughter is beneficial to the body and mind, which has long been established. However, if we examine domestic films, they are mostly martial arts films, supernatural films, social films, and erotic films: comedies are as rare as phoenix feathers. The so-called "toad wanting to eat swan meat" and the recently released "Chicken and Duck Couple" are examples. Directors seem to look down on comedies.

Moreover, in foreign films, even in non-comedies, there are often comedic interjections, which often make the audience laugh and lift their spirits. In domestic films, this aspect does not seem to be noticed either.

Given the continuous import of foreign comedies, will film companies run by Chinese people also awaken?

(2) After Watching "Chicken and Duck Couple"

— Gu Buwen

The day before yesterday, the Central Grand Theater distributed its flyers and published its advertisements to promote Liu Chunshan's "Chicken and Duck Couple," which was released in Shanghai. They spared no effort in promotion, saying things like "Chaplin's formidable opponent," "Warning to Lloyd Bacon to wake up," "S. Z. Sakall will laugh three times even with a straight face," and "Laurel and Hardy are so anxious that they dare not cheat." This kind of slogan, plus the title of the film, "Chicken and Duck Couple," literally means that it must be extremely funny. Therefore, it attracted me, a two-dollar moviegoer, to endure the pain of upgrading and join the ranks of four-dollar moviegoers. (Omission)

After watching these two Chinese comedies, I think we have not yet found a formidable opponent to resist Chaplin, nor is it enough to warn Lloyd Bacon to wake up. S. Z. Sakall may have three sarcastic sneers after watching it, and Laurel and Hardy may not understand it at all. In short, comedic expressions do not necessarily have to be slapstick. Originally, people's small movements and actions all have reasonable comedic situations. There is no need to be extremely fierce, make a scene, go crazy, chase, jump, and leap just to make the audience laugh, without any value for recollection. This is my loyal advice to Chinese comedies.

(3) Thoughts on the Future of Domestic Comedies

— Xing Su

Comedy films have their own art and position, and it is by no means simply making people laugh. They can go deeper than other films, piercing the depths of society or humanity. The reason why comedy films are not easy to perform and not easy to produce to the satisfaction of the audience is a definite reason. (Omission)

The performance of this "Chicken and Duck Couple" should be forgiven to some extent. Most of these actors are accustomed to singing on stage. Working in front of the camera is really the first time for them. They all lack experience, and there are many flaws. The directing and photography techniques are also too poor. The script is the same as other failed comedies, not escaping from being close to making a scene and absurdly bad. It will make people feel cold. After watching this "Chicken and Duck Couple," I thought about the future of domestic comedies. But I hope they will continue to work hard! (Omission)

A Brief History of a Star

A Brief History of Tallulah Bankhead's Childhood (Part 2)

— Mei Cun

One day, her golden hair braided into small braids, she ran into the house, breathing quickly. Her grandparents said, "When I grow up, I want to be an actress." Her discerning aunt did not argue with her about her mistakes; she adapted to the circumstances and allowed her curiosity to develop. Therefore, Tallulah often practiced graceful postures, wanting to prepare to become a star when she grew up.

However, she was still afraid of her grandparents' strict control, so she often thought of using a trick to escape this hateful family. She finally agreed with June to sneak away to a convent in Washington, D.C., where they were sent to study at St. John's College. In this college, she was the most beautiful girl.

After this naughty trick, fearing that her sisters would report her to her family, she wrote a long and pious letter to her grandparents, saying that she was willing to become a nun and live in the convent forever. At the age of fourteen, Tallulah graduated.

She said: "The education I received was ridiculous. I only chose to study what I liked the most, French. I was most impatient with arithmetic. It was simply a waste of time."

When Tallulah was seventeen years old, she made her debut in Washington. However, her father, Bankhead, had already become a senator, so he hoped that his beautiful daughter would continue her previous lovely social life, but Tallulah was unwilling.

Before she went to Washington, in her hometown, she once secretly sent her photo to a beauty contest. On the day of the announcement, she saw her photo published in a magazine, with a "?" mark underneath, because she wanted to keep it a secret, so she did not fill in her name when she sent it. This was the most exciting day of her childhood. In the contest, she had already won; therefore, her various future affairs were also decided.

She took the magazine and ran home, panting, and turned out the book to show her family, saying that she wanted to go on stage again to try it out. This was in 1918, and she was sixteen years old. Although she decided to become an actress, her family felt lonely because Tallulah left, and they did not approve of it.

Tallulah's father also had the idea of becoming an actor in his childhood, but he was finally persuaded by his parents to study law. Now, he cannot think of a way to change the will of his beautiful daughter.

Judging from the above, Tallulah's idea of becoming a star had already been formed in her childhood. In addition, she was not afraid of the obstacles of adversity, so she was able to achieve her current status, which is truly not an accidental thing. She is now thirty years old. Her fighting spirit continues to grow with age. If Marlene Dietrich returns to her country after her contract expires in December this year, then Tallulah has a good chance of winning the queen seat of Paramount next year. "Where there is a will, there is a way," this is also a clear proof. (The End)

As I See It

All Kinds of People in Movie Theaters

— Dao Sheng

There are all kinds of people in movie theaters, and they all have their own purposes. Now, let's briefly analyze them:

(1) Modern youths: They often go with the opposite sex, aiming to use the love stories in the films to promote the degree of their love.

(2) Wives: They are tired of watching Peking opera and supernatural stage plays, so they come to the movie theater to stroll around and adjust themselves.

(3) Gentlemen and merchants: Leisurely gentlemen and wealthy fat merchants watch one or two movies every week to relax and relieve boredom.

(4) Poor guys: Poor guys have no extra money to enjoy themselves. How can they be guests of movie theaters? However, according to my own experience, whenever I am troubled and cannot stand the boredom, I will go to a cheap movie theater to watch a movie. The purpose is to temporarily forget the pain and give the body and mind a moment of intoxication.

(5) Film critics: Film critics visit movie theaters with a mission, which is very different from the purpose of the above four types of people. They focus all their attention on the merits of the plot, the excellence of the directing techniques, the expressions of the protagonist and supporting actors, and other issues, in order to provide a basis for their reviews.

Monographs on Cinema

From Anger to Alarm

The third formula for practicing expressions alone is the transition from anger to alarm. In our first formula for practicing alone, the transition from blurred to attentive, the eye sockets have already widened a lot. In the second formula, the transition from attentive to anger, the eye sockets have doubled in size. Now, in the third formula, we gradually increase the glaring eyes of anger to the point where they cannot be increased any further, holding our breath, and even our mouths cannot be closed. This is the expression of extreme panic, which is also the expression of the extreme widening of the eye sockets.

Generally, when a person suddenly encounters a very terrible phenomenon and still has a little resistance, the eye sockets will naturally suddenly enlarge. This is a proper manifestation of the instinct of self-defense. However, when there is no way to resist or no strength to resist, the eye sockets will suddenly close. You see, when children are playing, they suddenly fall, and their eyes will close very tightly, as if they are afraid of death or waiting to die.

The practice method of the third formula is similar to the previous two formulas. First, put the eyes in a state of anger, and then inhale sharply, counting exactly eight numbers, and gradually widen the eye sockets to transition to a state of alarm. At the same time, the mouth also gradually enlarges to a state of gaping. Hold this breath and maintain this state, counting silently in your heart: "One, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight." Then, when exhaling this breath, gradually reduce the size of the eye sockets and mouth, returning to an attentive state. When exhaling this breath, also count silently from "one" to "eight" as before.

After continuing to practice three times, close your eyes and rest for one minute.
